Current Commentary

The Seriousness of the Bandit Situation in Northern Hebei

The North China War Zone: From the beginning of the takeover until today, more than a month has passed. After several obstacles and twists, it seems that it can be declared over in general terms. However, according to the reality, the five major passes along the Great Wall are still under the trampling of nomadic cavalry, and the remaining dozens of secondary passes are still occupied by enemy troops. Dushan and Xinglong are protruding beyond the customs, refusing to be returned. Linyu County is adjacent to the puppet territory, forcing relocation. Even in the counties that have been taken over, how can they get rid of the restraints of the Japanese? The number of troops stationed in Miyun is not decreasing but increasing. The construction of the airport in Zunhua is in full swing. Puppet troops are rampant in Yutian, and Chinese traitors are active in Tangshan. In other places such as Luanzhou, Qian'an, Jianchangying, and Shixia, there is no place where arrogant soldiers are not seen rampant. No administrative measure is free from Japanese interference. The so-called return is just a nominal reward. "The government is run by Ning, but the sacrifices are made by me alone." This is the biggest concession that the Japanese side considers.

However, the bad situation does not stop there. Recently, the bandit atmosphere in the eastern counties of Luanhe River has become increasingly rampant. They gather in groups and openly extort money. The area along the mouth is particularly rampant. Light and heavy machine guns, mortars, and field artillery, which are called new-style combat weapons, are all fully equipped. With this, they engage in plunder, and it is not surprising that they are in a state of being uncontrollable. In a war zone that has been occupied by the enemy for a long time, so many bandit troops suddenly appear. How can such despicable bandits in the mountains and forests possess such sophisticated weapons? From where does the supply and support come? Someone is behind the scenes, and it is about to be revealed. With a little thought, it is not difficult to understand. The county magistrates are on the border and are often held hostage, living like corpses with a dying breath. They have no vitality and can be knocked down with a finger. How can they withstand being destroyed? Dong Tianhua fled to Tianjin in a panic, and Zhang Gaichen broke through the encirclement and fled. This is what we expected. However, the Japanese news agency is using this opportunity to publicize and help the bandits spread their lies. It says that the order in Qin Island has fallen into chaos, or that Tangshan has been suddenly attacked by bandits. It says that the Japanese police in Yuguan have rushed to protect it, or that Song Naigan is discussing with the Japanese military commander. The fact that they want to create terror as a pretext for wrongdoing can be easily predicted from their past actions. The future crisis in North China is brewing in secret.

The reason why the Japanese are replaying the meaning of provocation this time is not necessarily due to the military returning to the old path, but can be regarded as a sudden diplomatic threat. Since the signing of the Tanggu Truce Agreement, after being complacent, the Japanese soldiers thought that our country would completely surrender and listen to their wishes. They also wanted to use this to end the military affairs and declare a complete victory. However, they suddenly heard that Song Ziwen had established a cotton and wheat loan in the United States and promoted technical cooperation in the League of Nations, which immediately made their suspicious eyes turn into flames of rage. In the past month, they have done everything possible to destroy technical cooperation. Since Luo Wengan's inspection of Xinjiang and Wang's proposal to concurrently serve as foreign minister, Japanese propagandists have been moved again, trying their best to promote the transformation of our country's foreign policy. At the same time, they are also singing high about preparing to welcome Song Ziwen's visit to Japan, intending to lure our country into their trap. However, Song's visit to Japan did not land, and all signs disappeared. This is a major disappointment for the Japanese. Because of disappointment, they become suspicious. Because of suspicion, they threaten, drawing swords and bows, demanding alliances. Where will their wild ambitions and greed lead? All these speculations should not be completely false.

Knowing where the Japanese cunning plots lie, our government authorities must urgently seek countermeasures. How to use diplomatic means to resolve the current disputes, and how to coordinate resistance plans to ensure the security of North China, all of which should be gathered from collective thinking and acted upon immediately. If we still repeat the old mistakes of procrastination and sitting idly by, then the previous mistakes can be found again, and the disaster of biting the navel will be unavoidable. The people in the North China region who have survived the disaster have not recovered from their wounds, and the hidden pain is still strong. How can we bear to let them fall into an unfathomable abyss again?

Disaster Reports from Various Provinces

(Nanjing) From January to August of this year, a total of fourteen provinces have reported disasters such as earthquakes, floods, droughts, rats, locusts, soldiers, bandits, hail, black frost, and epidemics. The counties affected by the Yellow River breach this time are not included in the calculation. (1) Hunan: 42 counties affected by floods, 15 counties affected by droughts, and 1 county affected by bandits. (2) Henan: 20 counties affected by bandits, 18 counties affected by floods, 11 counties affected by droughts, 11 counties affected by hail, 40 counties affected by frost, 6 counties affected by locusts, and 18 counties affected by plagues. (3) Shaanxi: 18 counties affected by bandits, 14 counties affected by droughts, 31 counties affected by frost, 37 counties affected by wind, 40 counties affected by hail, 27 counties affected by floods, 1 county affected by droughts, and 1 county affected by epidemics. (4) Hubei: 16 counties affected by floods and 1 county affected by droughts. (5) Anhui: 1 county affected by bandits, 2 counties affected by wind, 4 counties affected by floods, and 2 counties affected by hail. (6) Gansu: 7 counties affected by earthquakes, 5 counties affected by bandits, 4 counties affected by droughts, and 1 county affected by epidemics. (7) Zhejiang: 11 counties affected by floods. (8) Jiangxi: 2 counties affected by bandits (counties occupied by bandits are not included in this list) and 16 counties affected by floods. (9) Hebei: 22 counties affected by floods. (10) Guizhou: 13 counties affected by droughts, 3 counties affected by hail, and 1 county affected by floods. (11) Fujian: 5 counties affected by bandits, 11 counties affected by droughts, 3 counties affected by floods, and 3 counties affected by wind. (12) Sichuan: 7 counties affected by soldiers and 10 counties affected by bandits. (13) Jiangsu: 1 county affected by floods. (14) Qinghai: 1 county affected by bandits. (30th dispatch)

They have negotiated with Wang and Xu Shiying to expedite urgent relief, and will telegraph Jiang, Song, and Kong Xiangxi to jointly seek relief. (30th dispatch)

Add Zhang Weicun to go to Beijing to request urgent relief. 3. Actively make cotton clothes with 100,000 yuan. Domestic Grain Sales Stagnant, Ministry of Railways Not Responsible

(Nanjing) The person in charge of the Ministry of Railways stated that the Ministry of Railways has reduced freight charges separately for grain transportation, but sales have not been smooth so far. The key is that foreign grain is imported duty-free and arbitrarily sold. Moreover, the freight policy and the tariff policy complement each other. If they are combined, the effect is great, and if they are separated, the effect is offset. Therefore, supporting domestic grain, especially the duty-free import of foreign rice, is a major issue. As for the various exorbitant taxes and miscellaneous levies in the inland, which are repeated and overlapping, they are also the biggest obstacles to transportation and sales. This matter is not under the jurisdiction of the Ministry and cannot be held responsible. (30th dispatch)

Zheng Case Under Investigation in Nanjing

(Nanjing) Niu Chuanchun in the Zheng Yuxiu case was tried by the criminal court of the Jiangning District Court at 10 am on the 30th. Niu and his defense lawyer Peng Wangzu appeared in court. The trial was conducted by Xu Bangzhi, the presiding judge of the criminal court. The court first asked the defendant's name, age, and address, and then asked the defendant a few questions. Then, the defendant's lawyer made a request, saying that although the defendant was a clerk, all matters were handled by the recorder Feng Quan. Please summon Feng for investigation. Feng originally lived in Shanghai, but his whereabouts are currently unknown. However, regarding the evidence that Feng worked in the local court, the three agencies of the Jiangsu High Court, the Judicial Administration Department, and the Auditing Department can obtain receipts for Feng's monthly salary by consulting the receipts and binding books of Zheng's tenure. The court ordered to grant the defendant's request to summon Feng Quan to court first, and then schedule a court hearing at a later date. (Central News Agency dispatch)

Chen Gongbo Discusses Feng's Recent Situation in Mount Tai

(Nanjing) Chen Gongbo, Minister of Industry and Commerce, returned to Beijing from Jinan on the morning of the 30th. According to him, this trip south from Peiping, passing through Mount Tai, and visiting Feng on the mountain was purely a private visit and had no political significance. The conversations were entirely about past events and the situation after a long separation. He did not talk about Feng's current or future matters. He had not heard of the rumor that the central government would appoint Feng as the Director of the Yellow River Water Conservancy or the Army Inspector. Feng had no prejudices against the central government's measures, and only expressed the possibility of coming to Beijing to participate in the Fifth Plenary Session. (30th dispatch)

(Xuzhou) Chen Gongbo passed through Xuzhou on the evening of the 29th and went south. According to him, the trip to the north was for inspection. The results of the Dingxian Experimental Village were quite good. Due to the unrestored security in North China, industry and commerce cannot be promoted for the time being. He met Feng when he passed by Mount Tai, and Feng seemed to be in very good condition. He may go to Beijing for a visit soon. (29th dispatch)

Duolun Puppet Troops Move West

Tang Department Hopes to Return to Song for Reorganization

Tan Division Temporarily Stationed in Wanquan Area

(Peiping) After the Tang Department occupied Guyuan, the Duolun Li Shouxin puppet troops have recently moved west. Baocheng County is currently garrisoned by Zhang Lisheng's cavalry, with a total of more than 12,000 soldiers. Kangbao is garrisoned by a detachment of Zhi Yinglin. There are too many local garrisons, and the supply is extremely difficult. Tang has repeatedly sent Chief of Staff Wang Hongru to contact Zhang, hoping to return to Song for reorganization. Song has telegraphed Peiping for instructions. Some of the reorganized troops in Chahar East, such as Liu Guitang and Huang Shouchong, are stationed in Chicheng and Dushikou. The local people have suffered greatly. The provincial government receives dozens of complaints every day. Tan Zixin's troops are temporarily stationed in the Wanquan area. It is reported that the Japanese and puppet troops in Duolun are commanded by the Japanese Ozu Yanagi. (30th dispatch)

Zhangjiakou Tan Zixin issued a circular on the 26th after taking office as the commander of the newly編制的陸軍騎兵第十師 (Provisional Tenth Cavalry Division of the Army): "To all newspapers, since the Northeast Incident, our territory has fallen, and the black waters and white mountains have disappeared in the smoke of gunpowder. Our elders and brothers are groaning under the iron hooves and golden spears. Since childhood, I have aspired to join the army. Fortunately, I have encountered opportunities and have held military positions. I have deeply resented the Japanese bandits and have been determined to save the country. Therefore, I have organized a brigade and raised the banner of resistance against Japan. I have united the loyal and righteous and fought for years. Although I have failed due to lack of resources, the enemy has also been exhausted. Although I have not been able to eliminate them in one morning, is it not gratifying to avenge the country by even a fraction? This spring, Rehe was in danger, and I rushed to help. Chengde was subsequently lost, and I held Chahar East. After the Tanggu Truce, Chahar suddenly changed. The swords were drawn, and the war clouds were filled. Fortunately, the central government's policy was generous, and He, Song, Pang and other gentlemen worked hard to resolve the crisis, turn swords into plowshares, end the war in North China, and bring peace to the people. The martial arts are subdued, and the whole world admires them. Because my division was stationed in Chahar Province, it was trapped in a whirlpool. The environment was oppressive, and I was indecisive for several months. However, I have never dared to abandon my loyalty to the party and the country. My sincerity can be testified by heaven and earth. Now that the military affairs of Chahar Province are over, our central government cherishes the labor of those who have suppressed rebellion and driven out the enemy. It wants to gather and train them to serve the same hatred. Therefore, it has ordered my division to be reorganized into the Provisional Tenth Cavalry Division of the Army, and Tan Zixin has been appointed as the commander. I am grateful and ashamed. I am clumsy and unqualified for this important task. I am afraid of falling short. However, because the country is in difficulty, I cannot refuse the duty. I will do my best to repay the kindness. I took office at the headquarters of the division in Kongjia Village on the day of Youri. From now on, I swear to lead my troops, serve the central government, work hard in training, and be ready for deployment. This will never change. I hereby telegraph this to you and hope that you will understand. Tan Zixin, Commander of the Provisional Tenth Cavalry Division of the Army, bows in gratitude." (30th dispatch)

Gasoline-Soaked Rafts Intended to Burn Puppet Gunboats

Suspected to be the Work of Righteous Soldiers

(Harbin) According to the information obtained by local officials today, someone intended to set fire to seven puppet gunboats that were anchored in Raohe (translation) on the 28th and have now returned to the Amur River. When the gunboats were anchored, rafts full of gasoline suddenly floated towards the gunboats' anchorage. The situation at the time was extremely dangerous. Fortunately, the gunboat personnel handled the situation properly and avoided any losses. Although it is rumored that this act was committed by anti-"Manchukuo" troops, all parties still believe that outsiders are in charge of this. Therefore, the method is novel, and such a huge amount of gasoline can be obtained in the border area. (29th Reuters dispatch)

Japanese Army Ministry Controls Resources of Eastern Provinces

Guidance Rights Directly Under Rikkawa

Supervisory Rights Transferred to Araki

Kwantung Hall to Reduce Scope

(Tokyo) Guidance for the development of industry in "Manchukuo" has always been carried out under the supervision of the Governor of Kwantung Hall, the Commander of the Kwantung Army, the Ministry of Colonial Affairs, and other related ministries. In this way, the monism of guidance in Manchuria cannot be thorough, and the establishment of national defense resource control in Japan and Manchuria has left some regrets. Therefore, the new policy being discussed by the leaders of the Ministry of the Army is: (1) Guidance rights are directly under the Commander of the Kwantung Army. (2) Supervisory rights are transferred to the Minister of the Army and the Prime Minister. (1) Reorganize and expand the Kwantung Army Special Service Department, and establish organizations such as the Economic Staff Headquarters directly under the Commander of the Kwantung Army. These opinions are relatively strong, so they are currently negotiating with related parties and seem to be implemented within the year. If so, the Kwantung Hall will have no relationship with the development of Manchuria, and the issue of reducing the size of the hall may be realized as a result. (30th Electric Communication Dispatch)

Japan Seeks to Stabilize Political Situation

Party-Government Cooperation Emphasizes Spirit, Not Formality. The Seiyukai's National Policies Gradually Seek Realization

(Tokyo) As a result of yesterday's meeting between Seiyukai President Suzuki and Prime Minister Saito, both sides expressed satisfaction. Prime Minister Saito reported the details of his meeting at the cabinet meeting, and each cabinet member also accepted the Prime Minister's opinion. The military department, which has always opposed compromise, has been very negative due to the attitude of the Seiyukai, and Army Minister Araki has also expressed opposition. If this continues, cooperation between the government and political parties may proceed smoothly, because both the military and financial groups believe that the current situation is very unfavorable to the struggle between the two groups. (30th Chinese Union Dispatch)

(Tokyo) The government has decided to gradually implement the national policies proposed by the Seiyukai through various government agencies. However, the government's opinion is not as strong as the Seiyukai's, and there is no intention to coordinate various national policies. They only want to use the spirit of national unity to overcome the difficulties of the extraordinary situation. In the future, the Seiyukai's policies will be used as a reference to create national policies, and no formal coordination will be made with the Seiyukai. If the government coordinates with the Seiyukai, it will have to obtain the consent of the Minseito Party first, and the different policies of the Minseito and Seiyukai may cause complicated problems. Now that the spiritual cooperation of Saito, Suzuki, and Wakatsuki has been established, the political situation can be said to be stable. The government is about to begin compiling the next year's budget. (30th Japan Union Dispatch)

Army Minister Araki Encourages Saito

Hoping to Establish National Policies

Enhance External Strength

(Tokyo) Army Minister Araki met with Prime Minister Saito after yesterday's regular cabinet meeting, continuing the previous discussion on domestic and foreign issues, especially regarding the US policy towards Japan after the breakdown of the World Economic Conference, and the active plans and facilities of a certain country towards Japan. Based on the information obtained by the military, he explained, and said that in half a year, Japan's foreign relations may encounter a major crisis, which is not impossible. He hoped that the government would work harder to establish countermeasures, and that it was urgent to act, demanding the Prime Minister's efforts. At the same time, they exchanged opinions on the Seiyukai's five major policy issues. (30th Electric Communication Dispatch)

(Tokyo) Prime Minister Saito met with Army Minister Araki for an hour after yesterday's cabinet meeting, reporting the details of the meeting of the three party leaders (Suzuki, Wakatsuki, and Adachi) and the content of the national policies proposed by President Suzuki. Araki expressed to Saito that the military was also very satisfied and encouraged Saito to make further efforts to serve the country. Army Minister Araki's opinion is very noteworthy. Originally, the military opposed political parties and their financial backers. When Saito and Takahashi invited Suzuki to join the cabinet, Araki advised Saito not to succumb to political parties, even if it meant a war. Major General Tanaka Kunishige, president of the Meirin Association, also advised Saito not to cooperate with political parties, and if political parties dared to cause trouble, he would be willing to support the government. In this environment, cooperation between the Seiyukai and the government seemed difficult to achieve satisfactory results. Unexpectedly, both the military and financial departments expressed satisfaction. The shift in the Japanese political atmosphere is to increase its strength to resist foreign countries. The following remarks made by Army Minister Araki are worthy of attention by both Chinese and foreigners: Although I have not read the policies proposed by President Suzuki, the meeting between the three party leaders and Saito is an undeniable fact. It is difficult to predict the outcome. The trend of the political situation has passed a new stage. No matter who is in this increasingly urgent situation, they should have considerable awareness, abandon all private rights, and look at the Prime Minister's determination. It is also possible to understand that all cabinet members are running the country with sincerity and enthusiasm. There will be considerable achievements in three months. (30th Chinese Union Dispatch)

Opportunities for Party Liaison Unripe

(Tokyo) The Seiyukai presented a general outline of its policies to the Minseito Party and the Kokumin Domei yesterday (the same as those presented to the government), aiming to create opportunities for party liaison. However, the Minseito Party did not attach importance to this matter. Secretary-General Egita claimed that even if the Seiyukai proposed setting up a joint political affairs investigation agency, our party would never agree. Therefore, the general trend of the Minseito Party is that it cannot readily follow the Seiyukai's persuasion. Therefore, although the Seiyukai is negotiating with them, there is little chance of it being realized. In fact, there are those within the Minseito Party who advocate liaison and have the same views as the Seiyukai. There have been repeated meetings. Once the political season arrives this autumn, there is a possibility that opportunities will develop rapidly. However, the Kokumin Domei, on the one hand, takes economic control as its fundamental policy, so its policies are different from those of the Seiyukai. It has already stated that it cannot agree. Yesterday, when the Seiyukai representative met with President Adachi, he added that the Seiyukai expects that there will be times in the future when it will have to oppose the government. Please understand the Minseito Party and the Kokumin Domei. These words have profound meaning. (30th Electric Communication Dispatch)

U.S. Government Revises Gold Ban

Permits New Mine Gold to be Shipped Abroad

Private Gold Holdings Under Treasury Control

Hyde Park – President Roosevelt today, via executive order, revised the gold ban, permitting newly mined gold to be transported abroad under the strict supervision of the Treasury Department. Simultaneously, all privately held gold in the country will be placed under the control and supervision of the Treasury Department's Internal Revenue Service. (29th National Telegram)

Hyde Park – President Roosevelt today abolished a portion of the ban on gold exports, permitting the Treasury Department to receive and the Reserve Banks to handle sales of new U.S. mined gold. He also decreed that those holding gold coins, bars, and certificates must report the amount held within two weeks, along with the reasons why currency could not be substituted. This lifting of the ban gives U.S. mining companies the opportunity to obtain higher prices. U.S. gold will primarily be sold to foreign buyers, then to those with licenses for gold use in the arts, industry, or professions. The sale price will be determined by the Treasury Department after considering transportation and insurance costs, etc., and must be equal to the best price available in the open global gold market. Regulations will permit the Treasury Department to issue licenses for those using gold for foreign trade or withdrawing cash from domestic banks, except for amounts under one hundred dollars. Anyone or any group, except for Reserve Banks, must obtain a license to use cash. After thirty days, no one is allowed to hoard gold coins, bars, or certificates, with penalties of ten thousand dollars and ten years in prison for violations. This order to relax the ban was suddenly announced today as the President left the White House by automobile. After this news spread, gold mining stock prices on the New York Stock Exchange rose sharply. Domestic gold stocks rose fifteen dollars, reaching a new record of over three hundred dollars, while others rose one to three dollars. The Treasury Department expects the U.S. gold mining industry to profit an additional fifteen million dollars per year as a result, and the resumption of business activity is expected. (29th Reuters Telegram)

Government Controls Gold Management – According to a statement from the White House in Summer time, this order does not permit the free circulation of gold, nor will it affect the government's gold reserves. According to the order, mine owners wishing to export newly produced gold must report to the Treasury Department. After reviewing the situation and deeming export permissible, the Federal Reserve Bank will handle the export on behalf of the mine owners, and after deducting transportation and insurance costs, etc., will return the proceeds to the mine owners. Therefore, the Treasury Department not only retains the right to purchase newly produced gold at the official price of $20.67 per ounce, but also has the power to approve or deny exports. Mine owners who wish to sell gold abroad must not only entrust the government with sales, but cannot independently decide on the amount to be sold. Furthermore, this order does not permit the establishment of a free trading market, nor does it diminish the government's control over gold.

Intended to Support the Gold Mining Industry – The government's intention in issuing this order is to support the gold mining industry, as the current overseas gold price is approximately nine dollars higher per ounce than the U.S. official price. Consequently, the industry has been advocating for permission to export newly produced gold for over a month. According to the industry's views, there are two factions: one, the so-called National Committee, advocates for establishing a free trading market in New York; the other, the American Mining Congress, believes that while a free market would benefit the industry, allowing the export of newly produced gold is closer to the government's monetary and recovery plans. Before issuing this order, the U.S. President consulted with both factions and adopted the export permission method.

Resisting British Monetary Policy – However, according to prominent bankers, the effect of this order is not only to encourage the gold mining industry. Since the beginning of July, Europe has repeatedly withdrawn huge amounts of gold from the United States. In the week ending August 5th alone, the gold shipped by the New York Reserve Bank to France was worth over 41 million dollars. The amount shipped to Czechoslovakia was also worth over 6 million dollars. Bankers are baffled by the fact that Czechoslovakia could have so much earmarked gold existing in the United States. Even the gold earmarked in New York for France is not numerous. The reason seems to be that Britain intends to assist the currency of European gold standard countries. Since setting up the Exchange Equalisation Account, Britain has had huge amounts of earmarked gold existing in New York. Although the government does not announce the amount shipped abroad, it is rumored that at least 140 million dollars have been exported recently, while imports are minimal. The government's permission for the export of newly produced gold is intended to replace this outflow of gold, which is killing two birds with one stone.

Gold Product Exports Restricted – Although there is a clause in today's executive order permitting the export of gold manufactured goods, a second order was issued placing this type of export under strict government control. It stipulates that the Treasury Department's Internal Revenue Service has full power to supervise all private gold holdings nationwide. For example, goldsmiths must report the amount of gold purchased from the government and the amount of gold jewelry and goldware manufactured to the Internal Revenue Service on a regular basis and be subject to inspection. Internal Revenue Service personnel can also prevent the domestic transportation or export of privately held gold coins and bars. Therefore, private gold hoarders will also be subject to strict government supervision.

Believed to Have Inflationary Effects – The impact of this order is not yet very apparent today. Those involved in securities trading seem to believe it has inflationary effects, so today's stock market is firm and prices are rising. In addition, commentators have different opinions. Inflationists claim it has inflationary effects, while others believe this claim is unfounded. (30th National Telegram)

U.S. Recovery Machine Picks Up Speed

Government Stores Huge Funds for Application

(Washington) – President Roosevelt's grand machine for national recovery is now accelerating its movement, aiming to achieve his work of injecting momentum into American agriculture and industry. At this time, the U.S. authorities have trillions of dollars stored for application. The largest expense is the $300 million public works program, while the smallest expense is the National Recovery Act, which is currently allocating only $250,000 from the $20.5 million in temporary emergency funds issued by the Treasury Department since July. The Treasury Department stores over $100 million in cash daily to cover the costs of recovery movements and ordinary administrative expenses across the country. To date, the Public Works Administration has spent a total of $120 million on construction matters. (29th Reuters)

It is estimated by General Johnson that 2 million unemployed people have regained work. Although national wages have increased by $30 million per week as a result, the full success of the recovery will only be achieved in two or three months. On the 28th, Central Committee member Zhang Ji of Xi'an arrived in Lintong from Tongguan in the evening. Due to rain and muddy roads, he stayed overnight at Huaqingchi. On the morning of the 29th, he departed from Lintong and arrived in Xi'an at 1:00 PM. He immediately went to the Preparatory Committee of the Xi'an Capital. According to Zhang's statement to the Central News Agency reporter, his visit was to inspect the construction of Xi'an, solicit opinions from the citizens of the accompanying capital, and propose a method to equalize land prices first to avoid monopoly. He also plans to visit the recent progress of the agricultural and forestry colleges and plans to establish the Huaxia Academy with Liu Shouzhong under Mount Hua to promote learning and arts in Guanzhong. Zhang plans to stay here for more than ten days before returning east. (Central News Agency dispatch from the 29th)

Difficulties in Handling the Aftermath of the Chahar Situation

Fang Zhenwu and Ji Hongchang Maintain a Strong Stance

Issuing a Circular Telegram Declaring Continued Resistance Against Japan

Fang Goes to Dushikou, Unsuccessful in Meeting Song

Duolun Lost Again, Chaotic Situation in Eastern Chahar

Zhangjiakou Correspondence: Regarding the handling of the aftermath of the Chahar situation, Song Zheyuan, after discussing the plan with He Yingqin and others in Beiping, returned to Chahar to implement it. There are three major principles regarding the reorganization of the army: (1) Fang Zhenwu, Ji Hongchang, and others will be given other titles and leave the army; (2) the troops of Fang, Ji, and other troops of Feng will be reduced in size and led by secondary generals; (3) all volunteer armies that have been reviewed and given titles by the military branch will be restored to their original structure. Under these three major principles, the reorganization of the miscellaneous troops in Chahar Province was started. Therefore, a specific plan was decided: (1) Fang Zhenwu will be given a title in the Military Affairs Commission or sent abroad with severance pay. His troops will be divided into three parts. Except for the two units of Bao Gang and Zhang Renjie, which will be reorganized separately, Fang's newly recruited troops will be reduced to two regiments, led by Ruan Xuanwu, who will be appointed as the commander of the Shangdu Garrison; (2) Ji Hongchang will be given the titles of military advisor and consultant to the Chahar Provincial Government, leaving the army. His troops will be reduced to two regiments, led by Zhang Yunrong, who will be appointed as the commander of the Zhangbei Garrison; (3) Zhang Renjie's unit of more than 10,000 people will be reorganized into the Provisional Third Division; (4) The old troops of Deng Wen, led by Tan Zixin, will be restored to the title of the 10th Cavalry Division; (5) Li Zhongyi's unit will be reorganized into the 24th Brigade, and Liu Zhendong's unit will be reorganized into the 25th Cavalry Brigade; (6) Liu Guitang's unit will be reorganized into a guerrilla force, and Liu will be appointed as the commander of the Eastern Chahar Guerrilla; (7) Sun Liangcheng's unit will be reorganized into two regiments under the control of Song, and Sun himself will be given another title. After Song returned to Chahar, he convened a meeting in Zhangjiakou with all parties concerned. The representatives from the military branch were Jiang Bocheng and Xiong Bin. The miscellaneous troops present were Ruan Xuanwu, Zhang Renjie, Tan Zixin, Li Zhongyi, Liu Zhendong, Sun Liangcheng, Zhang Yunrong, Tang Juwu, and representatives of Liu Guitang. Fang and Ji did not attend, and Ruan Xuanwu and Zhang Yunrong represented them. Pang Bingxun arrived in Zhang from Xuanhua. It is said that as a result of the meeting, most of the miscellaneous army generals agreed to the established plan. Ruan Xuanwu and Zhang Yunrong also indicated that they could accept the title of garrison commander. Sun Liangcheng tried his best to declare that he was willing to hand over military power and would no longer hold any title. However, Fang and Ji were tough in their attitude, so Ruan Xuanwu and Zhang Yunrong were recommended to separately persuade Fang and Ji. Zhang and Ruan left Zhang on the 25th with a mission and then received a telegram reporting that it was difficult to get to the point. Based on this, Song Zheyuan believed that the Japanese and puppet troops had invaded Duolun, and the situation in eastern Chahar was tense. He urgently sought to resolve internal problems as soon as possible to deal with foreign enemies together. Therefore, he decided to move the meeting place and personally went to Zhangbei to meet with Fang and Ji to discuss matters, following the example of the Shacheng meeting. Beforehand, he also sent a telegram to Fang and Ji, and Fang replied that he dared not trouble him. After receiving the telegram, Song still held a twelve-point enthusiasm and insisted on going. So on the afternoon of the 26th, at 1:00 PM, he, together with Xiao Zhenying and others, went to Zhangbei by car. However, before Song arrived, Fang led his guards and left Zhangbei first. Song arrived at 4:00 PM and saw that Fang had left. He immediately telegraphed Kangbao and Baochang to inquire and arrange a meeting, but Fang did not go there and his whereabouts were unknown. Therefore, Fang's whereabouts became erratic. It was not until tonight (27th) that a report was obtained, saying that Fang had gone to Dushikou, while Ji Hongchang was at Daqinggou. Song will temporarily stay in Zhangbei and still try to meet with Fang and Ji. If he is sure that he cannot meet them, he will return to Zhangjiakou and look for other ways. It is said that when Fang left Zhangbei, he issued a joint circular telegram declaring that he would continue to resist Japan, and his attitude was very firm. The various units of Fang and Ji are still holding high the banner of resisting Japan and have joined forces with Liu Guitang's unit to form a new front, which may be difficult to resolve satisfactorily for a while.

The puppet army of Li Shouxin re-entered Duolun a few days ago, but did not advance. However, Guyuan was invaded by Tang Yulin's troops again. Tang sent his chief of staff, Wang Hongru, to Zhangjiakou to explain his difficulties and request to be incorporated. On the other hand, he has close ties with the puppet army, which is the same attitude taken by Liu Guitang at the beginning of his entry into Chahar. Now, the puppet army in eastern Chahar is intermingled with the anti-Japanese army that automatically raised the banner, and the situation is even more chaotic than before. It is extremely difficult to clean up. The authorities, on the one hand, are holding a policy of appeasement and adopt a strategy of appeasement and pacification. On the other hand, they are deploying considerable forces to make the necessary preparations to secure the border. In addition to the original troops entering Chahar, Song's Feng division has all been concentrated in Zhangjiakou. Recently, Zhao Dengyu's division stationed in Shijiazhuang was transferred to Chahar. Zhao's troops arrived in Zhang today and transferred to Wanquan to take over the defense, and will advance forward in turn. (Dispatch from August 27th)

丨General Order for Military and Civilians to Cooperate in Apprehending丨

Nanchang Correspondence: Among the various bandit gangs, Zhu De and Mao Zedong are the brains behind the national bandits, issuing orders. The other bandit leaders are Fang Zhimin in eastern Jiangxi, who serves as the chairman of the Jiangxi-Northeast Pseudo-Revolutionary Committee; Kong Hechong in western Jiangxi, who serves as the commander-in-chief of the Pseudo-Sixth Army Corps; Li Tianzhu in western Jiangxi, who serves as the deputy commander-in-chief of the Sixth Army Corps; He Long in western Hubei; Zhang in southern Hubei; Shen Zeming on the border of Henan, Hubei, and Anhui; and Luo Huibing, the pseudo-commander of the 12th Army in northwestern Fujian, and Peng Dehuai, the pseudo-commander-in-chief of the 3rd Army Corps. Chairman Chiang recently reiterated the previous order for their arrest, stating that anyone who can capture the above bandit leaders alive or present their heads will be handsomely rewarded. A list of the bounties has been issued to all provincial commanders-in-chief and commanders, to all officers and soldiers, and announced to the entire country for joint cooperation in the apprehension. For Lin Biao, the pseudo-commander of the 1st Army Corps, and Dong Zhentang, the pseudo-commander of the 5th Army Corps, a reward of 80,000 yuan each for capturing them alive, and 60,000 yuan each for presenting their heads. For the pseudo-commander-in-chief Tang Zaigang, a reward of 50,000 yuan for capturing him alive, and 30,000 yuan for presenting his head.

For the bandit leader Kong Hechong in western Jiangxi, and the pseudo-commander-in-chief Cai Huiwen, a reward of 80,000 yuan each for capturing them alive, and 60,000 yuan each for presenting their heads. For the pseudo-deputy commander Li Tianzhu, a reward of 30,000 yuan for capturing him alive, and 20,000 yuan for presenting his head.

For the bandit leader Luo Binghui in western Fujian, and Peng Dehuai, the pseudo-commander of the 3rd Army Corps, a reward of 80,000 yuan each for capturing them alive, and 60,000 yuan each for presenting their heads.

For the bandit leader He Long in western Hubei, a reward of 80,000 yuan for capturing him alive, and 60,000 yuan for presenting his head. For the remaining pseudo-central committee members, pseudo-army corps political commissars, pseudo-army commanders, and pseudo-division commanders of the 1st, 3rd, and 5th Army Corps, a reward of 30,000 yuan each for capturing them alive, and 20,000 yuan each for presenting their heads. (August 28th)

Chiang Orders the Provinces Suppressing Bandits to Genuinely Organize the Baojia System

Cultivating the Basic Military Force of the People

Employing Gentry to Establish Local Corps

Nanchang Correspondence: Chairman Chiang believes that the provinces of Henan, Hubei, Anhui, Jiangxi, and Hunan, which are suppressing bandits, have been handling the Baojia system for years, often only seeking the appearance of completeness and not the implementation of the spirit, thus making the bandit suppression work completely entrusted to the army, and both political and civil power have failed. Now, a special plan for reorganizing the Baojia system and eliminating scattered bandits has been formulated, ordering the commanders-in-chief of all routes, all commanders, and the provincial governments to seriously improve the general shortcomings pointed out, cultivate the basic military force of the people, and follow the examples of Zeng and Hu to employ local gentry to handle local corps to assist the military and political forces where they cannot reach. The original text is as follows:

"It has been several years since the provinces have been handling the Baojia system. Examining its effectiveness, it is truly minimal. Examining the reasons, there are several points. First, there is no distinction between the urgency and the progress of the Baojia system. The Baojia regulations seem to be based on general situations on the surface, but in reality, the tasks of the Baojia chiefs and the strong men's teams are divided into normal and emergency situations. During the military progress, the urgency should be considered according to the time and place, and the measures should be different. For example, in the recovered areas, the Qingxiang (clearing the villages) should be carried out first. After the Qingxiang is somewhat successful, the self-defense should be organized. After the self-defense is sound, the Baojia system will be easy to organize and succeed. If the same steps are taken in different environments, it will inevitably be square pegs in round holes, and how can it be effective? Second, the methods of organizing the Baojia system are not flexible. The procedure for organizing the Baojia system should be to first organize the Baojia, select the Baojia chief, then stipulate the tasks, clear the population, formulate regulations, and compile the strong men, step by step. However, in the newly recovered bandit areas, the rural areas are destroyed, the people are displaced and have not returned, and the Baojia chiefs cannot be determined suddenly. An emergency organization should be implemented first for the existing people, and corresponding tasks should be assigned separately. After the local order is restored, the regulations should be followed and reorganized. The military should be assisted by the people's strength, and the politics should be able to advance side by side with the military. If the formal production of the Baojia chief is awaited before the preparation is made, the local order will not be restored for a day, and the Baojia system will not be completed for a day, that is, no one will be responsible for the place for a day, and it will be too late to waste things, and it will be difficult to achieve the effect of military-civilian cooperation. Third, the tasks of the Baojia system are not enforced effectively. The tasks of the Baojia system are originally to unite the people to resist foreign insults and clear the population to eliminate internal traitors, such as assisting the military police in searching and arresting bandits, building bunkers and roads, inspecting incoming and outgoing pedestrians, teaching the residents, and monitoring reactionaries. The Baojia regulations stipulate in detail, but the local governments do not understand the location of the tasks, only seek the appearance of completeness, and do not emphasize the implementation of the spirit. Often, the household registration is completed and the investigation is completed, and the gong can be assembled to be considered excellent performance. The viewpoint is already wrong, how can it be effective? To sum up these points, the essence of organizing the Baojia system is to revitalize the people's morale and eliminate bandits, but the enforcement is not effective, so that the bandit suppression work is completely entrusted to the army. If the army completely eliminates the bandits, then the Baojia system will never have a time to start, and both political and civil power will lose their effectiveness. Thinking of this, the future of bandit suppression is deeply worried. A special plan for reorganizing the Baojia system and eliminating zero bandits has been formulated, dividing the progress steps into three areas: Qingxiang, self-defense, and Baojia. In each area, the urgency is weighed, the main tasks are distributed, the key points of guiding the application of laws and regulations are stipulated, the deadline for implementation is stipulated, and the examples of Zeng (Guofan) and Hu (Linxiang) are followed to employ the gentry to handle the local corps to assist the military and political forces where they cannot reach. It is hoped that the military and political chiefs at all levels will learn from the past and deeply understand, supervise and urge the gentry and people to implement it earnestly, so as to achieve the effect of 30% military and 70% political. Do not treat it as a mere formality and repeat the same mistakes, causing delays. In addition to the separate orders, the plan is urgently sent to O copies, ordering them to follow, and to transfer and urge the subordinates to follow the same. This is the order."

Fujian and Guangdong Negotiate on Jointly Suppressing Bandits

丨The 19th Route Army Sends Representatives to Guangdong丨

Guangzhou Correspondence: The bandits in western Fujian recently captured Liancheng with the intention of seizing food. After the 19th Route Army advanced to suppress them, they repeatedly annihilated the bandits in the Mingkou area. The 60th and 78th Divisions have now approached the bandit area. The 78th Division Commander Qu Nian led two regiments on the 19th and recovered Xijiang. Recently, the 19th Route Army, in view of the impending large-scale offensive, needs to contact the friendly forces on the Guangdong border in order to achieve the effect of suppression. Therefore, Lin Zhuliang, the Chief of Staff of the 78th Division, was specially sent to Guangdong to negotiate everything with the Guangdong authorities. Lin arrived in the province on the 24th to discuss the matter of jointly suppressing bandits and coordinating with the Guangdong authorities, and requested that the military be sent 300,000 yuan in assistance for August. At the same time, he requested that the Guangdong authorities allow the recruitment of new soldiers for the 78th Division in Luoding and Yunnan counties in the West River to supplement the division. According to Lin, the defenses in western Fujian are now extremely solid. Cai Tingkai is in Longyan supervising the front line with three or four divisions of troops. Lu Xingbang's troops are stationed in Yong'an. Zhang Junsong's troops from the 234th Brigade of the Qu Division and Ma Hongxing's troops are deployed in the Anxi area. The 23rd Brigade of Yun Yinglin's troops has recently moved to Zhangping. Therefore, large armies are now gathered in the southwest of Fujian, and as soon as the opportunity arrives, the order to launch a general offensive will be given.

On the southern Jiangxi front, the bandits have recently attacked the defense areas of the official army in Sannan in order to contain the Guangdong troops supporting Fujian. On the 19th, about 700 bandits from the pseudo-7th, 8th, and guerrilla teams of Junmenling suddenly attacked the Hukeng defense line of the 1st Regiment of the 1st Army. The Wang Regiment of the unit sent out two battalions to fight head-on, killing more than 200 bandits before dispersing the bandits. In this battle, the female captain of the pseudo-8th Guerrilla Plainclothes Team, Weng Xiaozhen, was captured, along with seven male and female bandits. On the same day, more than a thousand bandits from the pseudo-20th Division gathered, along with a part of the pseudo-Worker Division, and were forced by the official army to flee to the highlands in the Xiaole and Yi areas, confronting Zhang Meixin's unit of the 4th Division of the official army. That morning, Li's regiment of Zhang's division advanced from Banshi to Shihou, and Kong's regiment advanced to the highlands in the eastern end of Xiaole, encircling the pseudo-20th Division. The bandits used machine guns and hand grenades to charge, and their momentum was very fierce. The two sides engaged in melee combat for an hour. Zhang's division increased the Xie battalion to the left wing, and the Li and Zhou battalions increased the right side, and the entire line simultaneously pounced, finally killing more than 300 bandits. The remaining bandits could not hold on and fled in disarray towards the Gaopai of Shuidong, leaving behind more than a hundred corpses, and the situation was extremely embarrassing. (August 25th)

Key News of Bandit Suppression in Fujian and Jiangxi

丨Frontline News from the Second Column of the Southern Route丨

Shantou Correspondence: Huang Renhuan, the commander of the Guangdong Army's Independent 1st Division, is currently the commander of the Second Column of the Southern Route Bandit Suppression Army. The division headquarters is located in Jiaoling, and a rear office is located in Shantou. (2) Zhang Meixin's division telegraphed from Anyuan that there were two or three thousand of the pseudo-Model Division in Qingxi, and more than a thousand bandits in Junmenling. The pseudo-Model Division and the pseudo-23rd Division had more than seven thousand. When the bandits defeated and returned to Tianxin Wei in Junmenling on the evening of the 10th, they ordered each person in the nearby townships to send five liters of rice, and claimed that there would be eight or nine divisions of people arriving soon. Also, the heavy stone, Shuidong, and Gaopai all had bandits who forced the people to collect grain and rice. At present, the counties of Chaozhou and Meizhou have announced martial law due to the rampant banditry in Fujian and Jiangxi, and are checking pedestrians and post and telecommunications day and night.
