Hanshan County Captured by Bandits

Neighboring Counties are Extremely Nervous

Wuhu Sends Troops to Assist in Suppression

Wuhu Correspondence: Hanshan County, Anhui, is a large county with the most abundant agricultural production and developed commerce in southern Anhui. It is located across the river from Wuhu, only tens of miles away. However, on August 26, several hundred bandits suddenly fled to the first town near the county seat, Xianzong, from Hefei. It is said that the bandit leader is Zhang Dabizi, who harassed Hefei and Shucheng and other places. They confiscated all the guns from the town's security team and plundered the entire town with great momentum. The county seat was very nervous and sent a security team out of the city to block them. However, the bandits disguised themselves as farmers, carrying sickles and other things, posing as refugees, and heading towards the county seat. They packed pistols and other equipment into packages and hired many elderly rural women to carry them on their backs and mixed them into the city. After the bandits approached the city walls, they began to attack fiercely at 4:00 AM on the 27th. Due to the lack of troops in the city, it finally fell around 10:00 AM. After the bandits entered the city, many displaced people joined them and first negotiated with the gentry, demanding a large sum of cash. Because they could not cope, they immediately released about sixty prisoners and then divided into streets to search door to door, while firing guns to show their power, densely like a string of beads. Until the evening, they kidnapped about two hundred and several dozen men and women hostages and retreated to the Xianzong Town and Huangshan Temple area. On the way, they released about a hundred hostages. However, it was heard that the wife and children of County Magistrate Wu Yinghan were all kidnapped, and the total loss reached tens of thousands of yuan. After this battle, the bandits captured a lot of guns and equipment, so the number of people also increased to more than a thousand. They spread the red army flag, and the surrounding counties, such as Chaoxian, Hexian, and Quanjiao, were all panicked. People fled to safe areas, and more people from Hanshan came to Wuhu to escape. In particular, Chaoxian County was in very critical situation. Wang Xianbao Zhai, the Administrative Inspector of the Second District of Wuhu, in addition to transferring a part of the first, third, and second companies of the security team to Chaoxian to assist in the blockade, also telegraphed the central government to quickly send large troops to suppress them to avoid spreading. (August 29th)

Hunan Province Piloting Cooperative Farms for Wounded Soldiers

The Provincial Government Allocates Two Thousand Acres of Official Wasteland

Aims to Provide Suitable Occupations for All Wounded Soldiers

Changsha Correspondence: Since the effective commencement of the year, the various divisions directly under the Central Government have mostly been formed by personnel recruited in Hunan. Therefore, there is no division without Hunanese. Currently, recruitment offices are still everywhere in Hunan. Vehicles transporting newly recruited soldiers are constantly on the road. Soldiers have become a special product of Hunan. In the event of casualties, the military authorities merely issue an order regarding the education of the wounded and the pensions for the deceased, with the entire burden falling on Hunan Province. He Jian once established the Fourth Route Army Disabled Soldiers' Rehabilitation Center in Xiangtan, which takes in disabled soldiers directly under He's Fourth Route Army, with funds drawn from national taxes. The Hunan Disabled Soldiers' Rehabilitation Center was established in Changsha, which takes in disabled soldiers sent back from various armies and divisions other than the Fourth Route Army, with funds drawn from provincial taxes. Currently, both rehabilitation centers are already full, and those who arrive later cannot be accommodated, leaving those turned away with no means of support. Each month, tens of thousands of dollars are spent on rehabilitation fees, but it only provides care and not education. In addition to eating without working, the wounded soldiers also have various special rights. All theaters, large and small, have special seats for wounded soldiers for their free entertainment. If citizens of Changsha have weddings, funerals, housewarmings, or birthday celebrations, the wounded soldiers will hold a red card, set off a string of firecrackers, and demand money. Each household is asked for a few dollars at a minimum, and tens of dollars at a maximum, not stopping until their goal is reached. The wounded soldiers have become a special class in Changsha society. As for pensions for the wounded and deceased, according to Chen Rujin, the director of the National Tax Revenue and Expenditure Office, who manages the allocation of pension funds from national taxes, the amount has been increasing year by year. In the 19th year of the Republic, only 134,044 yuan, 1 jiao, and 7 fen were spent on pensions. In the 20th year, 438,028 yuan, 4 jiao, and 5 fen were spent. In the 21st year, 504,975 yuan, 6 jiao, and 1 fen were spent. In the 22nd year, up to the end of June, it had increased to 800,693 yuan, 8 jiao, and 4 fen. Although there are no statistics for the amount of pension funds paid from provincial taxes, it is roughly equal to the national taxes. Furthermore, in the recent wars against Japan and the suppression of bandits, there have been even more casualties among Hunanese officers and soldiers. In the future, education and pensions will be even more complicated. Chen Rujin, who manages the national tax revenue and expenditure, believes that rather than spending large sums of money each month and letting them eat without working, it would be better to find a way to make them productive. He proposed to He Jian to pilot a cooperative farm for wounded soldiers. The provincial government would allocate two thousand acres of official wasteland to pilot one village first, with a temporary limit of fifty households, and then gradually expand. The required expenses would first be paid by the National Tax Office, and then deducted from the pensions due to the wounded soldiers, so that the wounded soldiers could gradually return to farming. He Jian considered it feasible and appointed Zhang Kailian, the Director of Finance, Yu Jichuan, the Director of Construction, Liu Yunsheng, the Director of the General Headquarters Medical Department, and Chen Rujin to actively prepare and agreed on a general outline of the plan as follows: (1) In order to provide suitable occupations for wounded soldiers and to turn pensions into productive uses, 20,000 yuan will be pre-allocated from the annual pension fund to pilot a cooperative farm for wounded soldiers. All wounded soldiers belonging to the Fourth Route Army who receive pensions annually from the national tax and who are physically able to farm and willing to return to farming, and approved by the Fourth Route Army Headquarters, may join the cooperative farm and cultivate land. (2) The land needed for the cooperative farm for wounded soldiers will be allocated two thousand acres of official wasteland by the Hunan Provincial Government. The start-up costs, as well as houses, farm tools, roads, ditches, will be paid in advance by the Customs Revenue and Expenditure Office. A separate budget will be drawn up in accordance with the cooperative system and recorded in the accounts of each wounded soldier. In the future, the wasteland will be cultivated and taxed according to law. The price of the land will be assessed according to the market price based on the amount of pension received by each wounded soldier. The land will be allocated accordingly, and the land price will be deducted from the pension due. Then, the government will separately issue management licenses to determine property rights. (3) All wounded soldiers who volunteer to return to farming must first be trained for six months in a designated agricultural vocational school or farm to acquire general agricultural knowledge before joining the cooperative farm. (4) In addition to ordinary crops, the cooperative farm for wounded soldiers should also focus on beekeeping, chicken farming, animal husbandry, and tree planting, so that wounded soldiers with incomplete limbs can also work. (5) The cooperative farm for wounded soldiers should organize production and consumer cooperatives separately. All purchases and sales, water conservancy projects, and new agricultural tools in the village should be operated in a cooperative manner. The regulations will be formulated separately. (6) All wounded soldiers who join the cooperative farm should live with their families to live and work in peace and be permanent. (7) The cooperative farm for wounded soldiers will be supervised and managed by a Hunan Wounded Soldiers Cooperative Farm Management Committee organized by one commissioner each from the Provincial Government, the Fourth Route Army Headquarters, and the National Tax Revenue and Expenditure Office. (8) The staff handling the cooperative farm for wounded soldiers will be temporarily transferred from relevant agencies during the pilot period and will not be paid salaries. (9) During the pilot period, the cooperative farm for wounded soldiers will temporarily operate one village, limited to fifty households. It will be promoted when it is successful. The above are general points. The detailed plan is still under discussion. The official wasteland required is said to be allocated from the newly silted land inside the Linxiang Yongji Dike. It is decided to complete the preparations in the shortest possible time so that spring farming can be carried out next year. (August 20)

Inspection Notes on Jiangxi, Anhui, Hunan, and Hubei by Our Correspondent Ren An

Cihua Town After Six Years of Banditry

Special Dispatch from Yichun: The Ganxiang Road starts from Nanchang in the east and ends at Pingxiang in the west, with a length of about six hundred li. Although it has recently been opened to traffic, the crushed stone pavement has not been completed in many places, and the junctions between the bridge ends and the dirt roads often form ridges of one or two inches in height, causing the car to bump greatly. Passengers must hold on tightly to the seat board, and if they lose their grip, they will inevitably hit their heads on the roof of the car. When passing through the three rivers of Xujiadu, Luxi, and Yuanhe, because the bridges are currently under construction, passengers must hire a ferry to change vehicles and buy tickets separately, which is particularly troublesome.

Yichun, formerly known as Yuanzhou, is a city on the upper reaches of the Yuan River, surrounded by green mountains, and the scenery is pleasant. The county's output is sufficient to supply itself, and the distribution of land is generally even. There are very few landlords with more than one hundred acres of land. Self-cultivating farmers and semi-self-cultivating farmers account for the majority of farmers. Therefore, when the Red Peril spread to the surrounding areas in the 16th and 17th years of the Republic, Yichun was able to enjoy temporary peace, which is a good reason. Later, the officials and gentry were too optimistic and failed to take precautions, which led to the gradual growth of the Red Bandits. In the 18th year of the Republic, they dared to capture the city with only two hundred miscellaneous guns. Later, they took the opportunity to successively capture neighboring cities such as Fenyi, Wanzai, and Anfu. By the beginning of the 19th year, when they captured Yicheng again, their guns had increased to thousands. Peng Dehuai served as the commander and was quite unstoppable. After Peng's bandits withdrew, although the National Army was stationed there, their strength was only enough to defend the city. They had no time to take care of the surrounding areas, so important bandit nests such as Cihua Town (the location of the Red Bandit Yichun County Soviet) and Fengdingshan have not yet been completely recovered.

Cihua Town is located in the center of the Sixth District, which protrudes from a corner of the county's border. It is about one hundred and twenty li from the county seat and the borders of Fenyi, Wanzai, Liuyang, Pingxiang, and other counties. The banditry has been going on for almost six years, and the foundation seems to be relatively stable. The Eighteenth Division once attacked it, but then withdrew. Later, the Sixty-second Division recaptured it and severely punished its banditized soldiers and civilians, destroying its various constructions, such as the Soviet government, Lenin Elementary School, Mint, Cooperative, and Textile Factory. They rebuilt solid and tall watchtowers and various defensive fortifications. After the completion, the division, because the area was surrounded by mountains on all sides, making transportation difficult, and it was inconvenient to station heavy troops, transferred the guard duty to the carefully selected local militia, encouraging them to take on the difficulty. Currently, the bandit area surrounding Cihua is about one hundred li in diameter, and the area guarded by the local militia is only about four li in diameter. The required salt, rice, and bullets must be sent in by outside teams. The fortifications are often in danger of being counterattacked by the bandits. To avoid the intense shooting from the high ground by the defending troops, the bandits often cover their heads with wooden boards covered with cotton quilts and move forward, rushing towards the fortifications, stacking them to form ladders, and engaging in close combat. However, because of the unfavorable terrain and insufficient ammunition, they suffered heavy casualties and retreated in embarrassment. Ouyang, the head of the Sixth District, served in the bandit area for five years, and his family was almost completely killed by the bandits. He was not subdued and vowed not to coexist with them. At the time when the district head resigned due to an event and returned to the city, the reporter, because he had dealt with the bandits for a long time and should be more familiar with the bandit situation, was introduced by the county government to meet and talk. According to him, "The Red Peril has spread throughout the territory, and the Sixth District is particularly red. Since the initial recapture of Cihua, everything about the bandit party's meeting ceremonies, slogans, doctrines, and meanings, if asked of old men and children, they can answer fluently without being held guilty. The bandit army's organization is roughly divided into the Red Army, the Young Pioneers, the Red Guards, the Guerrilla Team, the Search Team (investigating local tyrants and secret agents), the Transportation Team (lurking in the countryside or setting up tea houses along the way to communicate with each other and spy on enemy information), the Spear Team (the task is roughly the same as the Guerrilla Team, but the weapons are mostly spears), and the Comfort Team (composed of young women, specializing in comforting the victory of various teams and inducing the enemy to surrender). The slogans used to lure the people to join the Red Army are mostly 'Joining the Red Army is to find a way out for our proletariat, and joining the White Army is to be a running dog for the bourgeoisie. Although we have no weapons, in the future all weapons will belong to us,' etc. The land policy is that regardless of men, women, old, or young, each person has twenty-five grabs (about one mu), and the rest belongs to the Soviet government. The type of crops to be planted and when to plant them must be obeyed. Those who are lazy will be severely punished. If a large number of Red Army soldiers come, each person must supply a sheng of grain. If they do not have enough to eat, they must do other work to make up for it. Men and women who are physiologically unsound or have hereditary diseases are not allowed to marry. Those who are not married but are suspected of cohabitation are sentenced. Those who commit financial fraud, even if the amount is only one yuan, are also sentenced to death. Those who privately bury money underground are also killed. The silver coins they mint are the same in style and weight as the large foreign coins on the market, but the quality is mostly melted jewelry, so the color is slightly green. The villagers do not know, and some occasionally use them. The life of the bandit army is already extremely difficult on weekdays. Now, in the face of encirclement and blockade, the predicament is even more extreme. From now on, the military and civilians will cooperate and work hard to advance and eliminate the bandits. The bandits will have nowhere to flee and it will not be difficult to wipe them out in one fell swoop," he said. (August 14)

Jinpu Railway Robbery Case

Train No. 9 Robbed by Bandits in Qingxian

Railway Police Officer Shot and Killed by Bandits

Jinan Correspondence: On the 27th, Jinpu Railway train No. 9 from Tianjin to Jinan was robbed by bandits in Qingxian, Hebei Province, at 8:30 pm. The loss was more than 400 yuan, not including clothing, etc. The train was originally scheduled to arrive in Jinan at 7:00 am today (the 28th), but it arrived at 11:00 am due to the robbery. The details of the robbery are as follows:

Jinpu Train No. 9 left Tianjin Nankai yesterday morning (the 27th) with locomotive No. 106, two guard cars, twelve freight cars, two third-class cars, and two iron boxcars. In addition to more than 300 passengers in the third-class passenger cars, it was also fully loaded with various goods. There were no other incidents along the way after leaving Tianjin. At 8:30 pm, when passing through Qingxian, Hebei Province, more than a dozen passengers dressed in plain clothes bought tickets and boarded the train. They entered the third-class car, and two of them went directly to the top of the freight car. No one paid attention to them. After passing the first flag station of Qingxian, two bandits climbed from the top of the freight car to the locomotive, took out their hidden handguns, and forced the driver to slow down. Five or six bandits simultaneously surrounded the security team in the second-class car. The escort team accompanying the train was the sixth members of the fifth team of Jinpu Railway Security Force, led by squad leader Zhang Mingxi, plus three passengers. It had two rifles. There were three people in the iron boxcar, also with only two rifles. The police in the third-class car, seeing the large number of bandits, were helpless. At that time, Liu Shicai, a railway police officer in the third-class passenger car, saw that the situation was critical and was about to draw his gun to shoot the bandits, but he was spotted by the bandits, who immediately shot him. The bullet passed through his chest and he died immediately. A passenger next to him also suffered a minor leg injury. After the railway police officer was killed, the bandits took his gun. The remaining police officers hid in the corners of the car and dared not intervene. Then, after passing the third flag station of Qingxian Station, the bandits suddenly fired three shots. As soon as the gunfire stopped, more than a dozen hidden bandits with guns boarded the train. It turned out that the bandits had ambushed a group of bandits by the roadside of the third flag station when they boarded the train in Qingxian. After the ambushing bandits boarded the train, they entered the third-class passenger car and, together with the bandits in the car, rummaged through boxes and chests, searching extensively. They searched for more than 400 yuan from all the passengers, and all the straw hats and gowns were seized. However, all the luggage was not taken away. At Sanji, the bandits gathered, shouted, and got off the train, changed into straw hats and gowns, and dispersed separately. After the bandits left, the train continued south. Liu Shicai's body was carried down at Xingji. The injured passenger also got off the train at Cangzhou. The fifth team also changed shifts, and squad leader Ji Deshun of the sixth security team led the team to escort the train. The train arrived in Jinan at 11:00 am today (the 28th). (August 28)

Wuhu Workers Petition to the Instructor

Zhang Jun Explains the Reason for the Establishment of the General Labor Union

Wuhu Correspondence: The labor movement in Wuhu has been stagnant for a long time. Recently, the Anhui Provincial Party Department suddenly announced the appointment of Yang Gancheng, Pan Renzhong, and seven others as organizing committee members of the Wuhu General Labor Union, and appointed Zhang Jun as the instructor of labor organizations. Zhang arrived here the day before yesterday. After the members of the organizing committee were appointed, they also prepared to start work. Yesterday, workers from the Yuzhong Yarn Factory, Qizihua Industry, Shoe Industry Outsourcing, South Bank Wharf, Rice Milling and Hulling Workshops, and other labor unions, after the announcement of the labor organizing committee, in addition to preparing a document to request higher authorities, especially led thousands of workers in a procession to the Southeast Hotel on Zhongshan Road to petition the instructor Zhang Jun. After Zhang responded to the public, he briefly stated that "The intentions of all the workers have been understood. The reason why the province established the General Labor Union this time is that Commander-in-Chief Chiang previously convened a meeting of the Party committees of four provinces in Lushan. Regarding mass organizations, he advocated practical training to revive the mass movement, so the Provincial Party Department urgently established the Wuhu General Labor Union. As for the organizing committee members who are not suitable, I will of course be responsible for submitting a request to the Provincial Party Department to replace them. Please trust and forgive everyone." Finally, all the workers shouted slogans and dispersed. (August 26)

Nantong

Martial Law Implemented in the Four Townships to Guard Against Bandits

There have been disturbances by scattered bandits in the coastal areas of Tongyi, and bandits in the four townships have also been active recently. Because there were rumors that bandits were robbing police weapons, the county government ordered the police and local militia in each district to be on strict alert. The provincial water police team is responsible for inspecting all ports. The Provincial Security Regiment stationed in Tong, due to the unrest, has decided to launch a large-scale search and suppression.

Changshu

Impersonating a Military Officer to Widely Send Wedding Invitations Leads to Arrest

Zhou, who lives in Qinglong Lane in the city, recently had a whimsical idea and widely sent out wedding invitations, saying that his son was one year old and he would be hosting a banquet at home on the 31st of this month. The invitations included a photo of "Cadets of the Sixth Class of the Central Army Military Academy." The county magistrate, the director of the public security bureau, and various staff members were all on the list of those invited. After receiving the invitation, County Magistrate Zhou Heng believed that this must be a false name used to swindle and deceive, and ordered the Public Security Bureau to go to the address to arrest him. As a result, Zhou Yong, who was impersonating a military officer, was arrested, along with many congratulatory gifts and thank-you notes. Huang Cheng, the judge, opened a court for questioning. According to his confession, his name was Zhou Yong, also known as Zhou Yuanjin. He used to work in a rice shop and now sells radish pancakes. He has no wife or children. Because life was difficult, he resorted to this strategy and asked to be exempted from prosecution. The official Yu, considering that it was a first offense, leniently sentenced him to two months of imprisonment.

Gaoyou

Water Police Soldiers Commit Violence

On the 26th, soldiers of the provincial public security team stationed in Ershilipu suddenly went to Cheluo Town for unknown reasons, arrested Li Wei, a reporter from the Huaihai News, and the mother of the town's mayor, beat them severely, and their lives were in danger. The merchants and residents of the entire town were extremely indignant at the team's illegal actions and went on strike on the 27th. Currently, the families have sent the victims to the county to examine their injuries and request that they be severely punished.

Jiangyin

Request to Stop Collecting Winter Grain Transport Surcharge

The case of collecting two yuan per stone of grain transport in the winter in Jiangsu Province originated in the era of the warlord Sun Chuanfang. After the National Army established itself in Jiangnan, it was changed to a one-year limit and no longer collected. Unexpectedly, there have recently been moves to extend the collection. The Jiangyin County Chamber of Commerce, Relief Institute, Public Property Office, and other institutions, believing that at a time when people's livelihoods are declining and low grain prices are harming farmers, this collection should no longer be made to increase the burden on the people, sent a telegram to the Executive Yuan, the Ministry of Finance, and the Chairman of the Province on the 28th, requesting an immediate order to stop it in order to eliminate harsh levies.

Wuxi

Police Officer Tramples Villager to Death While Arresting Gamblers

Wang Xuehan, a patrol officer from the Third Branch of the Eighth Branch of the Public Security Bureau in Hua Dafang Village, District 13 of the county, sent police chief Wang Baode and six police officers, including Zhu Yunshi, to arrest gamblers in Chen Xinggen's teahouse in Hetanqiao. They arrested two gamblers, He Dongyuan and others. Later, they went to the teahouse opened by Lu Runzhang in Yuanlongqiao to arrest gamblers and arrested three gamblers, Lu Sanduo and others, and took them to the station. Unexpectedly, during the arrest, they trampled the villager Zhao Xinggen to death. When Officer Wang learned of this, he sent the police officer, along with the gamblers, to the Eighth Branch, and Chief Liu sent them to the County Public Security Bureau yesterday. At the same time, Tu Zheng came to the city to report to the County Court, requesting that someone be sent to examine the body for verification and handling.

Kiln Industry Asks to Be Exempted from Business Tax

The Brick and Tile Kiln Industry Association of the county, as well as the Linong Brick and Tile Company, Gongda Brick Factory, and Yunli Lime Factory, etc., due to the Jiangsu Lime, Brick, and Tile Kiln Business Tax, the Wuxi Collection Office of the Third District collects business tax according to the estimated turnover, temporarily charging 5% of the interest rate of two cents, which is more than four times higher than the original 0.5% of the capital amount. Moreover, regardless of whether the goods produced have been sold or shipped from the factory, the tax is based on the output as the tax standard. It is called business tax, but in reality, it is even harsher than the factory tax. The industry cannot bear the burden, so yesterday they jointly sent a letter to the County Chamber of Commerce, requesting that it be forwarded to the Department of Finance to order the collection office to exempt them from the tax in order to maintain a glimmer of livelihood, and also requested that it be forwarded to the Department of Construction for assistance.

Xiaoshan

Bandits Intercept and Rob Night Boats

The night boat from Linpu to Kanshan set sail from Kanshan on the 27th, fully loaded with goods, and returned to Linshan. When it reached Tingtou Bridge near Suoqian, at dawn, nine bandits suddenly came, fired shots, and ordered the boat to stop. They jumped into the cabin and carried out a wanton robbery, stealing more than 40 yuan of silver, and many items of clothing from the boat crew.

Merchants in Southern Township Plan to Set Up a Paper Mill

Shen Qizhou, a merchant from Tangcunban Village in Southern Township of Xiaoshan, has been an assistant manager in a paper mill in Shanghai. Recently, he saw that the paper troughs in Wu Xiao are all adhering to the old methods and do not know how to improve, so that foreign paper is imported and the sales of local paper are declining day by day. In order to recover the rights and interests and revitalize domestic products, Shen has decided to open an improved paper mill in his village. He specializes in imitating various kinds of foreign paper and is currently consulting with nearby paper troughs in order to raise shares to open the mill.

Yixing

Request for Exemption from Winter Grain Transport Surcharge

Yiyi was forced to borrow one year of winter grain transport during the time when Sun Chuanfang was the governor of Jiangsu. In the winter of the 19th year of the Republic, it continued to be collected in the name of the Northern Expedition. With the approval of Ye Chuqia's administration of Jiangsu, a surcharge of two yuan per stone of grain transport was collected for a period of one year. The people endured the pain and paid it off. In the 20th and 21st years, it was continued to be collected again by analogy. Up to now, it has not been exempted. If this continues year after year, it will inevitably become a permanent land tax surcharge. At a time when there have been frequent years of famine and the rural areas are bankrupt, it is difficult to cope with the regular tax, let alone the extra surcharges. Therefore, the County Organizing Committee, the Chamber of Commerce, the Journalists Association, the Farmers Association, the Education Association, the Public Property Management Office, the Education Bureau, and Zhu Zhongjing, the district heads of all fourteen districts in the county, sent a telegram to the National Government, the Executive Yuan, and the Ministry of Finance on August 29, appealing to them to quickly order the Jiangsu Provincial Government to permanently stop the collection of grain surcharges and not continue to collect them by analogy, in order to alleviate the people's difficulties.

Huzhou

Two Bandits Shot Dead While Resisting Arrest

In Taiyang Township, Daixi, Southern Township of Huzhou, there was a farmer named Zhang Jianmao, whose family was well-off, which was coveted by bandits. Unexpectedly, at about 11 pm the day before yesterday, a number of bandits speaking Hakka suddenly came, each holding a handgun, broke into the house, and carried out a large-scale robbery, stealing eight carts of fine silk, one Dao gun, and clothing and jewelry, etc., causing great losses. The Second Regiment of the Huzhou Security Team stationed in Daixi learned of this and immediately ordered ten soldiers from the team to rush to pursue and arrest the bandits. The bandits opened fire to resist, and the soldiers also returned fire. After about an hour, the bandits were unable to hold out and fled in all directions. Two bandits, Zhang Dezhu and Qian Dedang, were shot dead on the spot, and all the stolen goods were recovered.

Two Women Fight and Cause a Death

Wang Jiang, a woman from Daixi Town, had a verbal argument with Yang Shi, also from the town, a few days ago, which led to a fight between the two. Wang Jiang was seriously injured by Yang Shi and died on the afternoon of the day before yesterday. The family of the deceased reported to the police station in the town. After receiving the report, Director Ruan ordered the police to arrest Yang Shi and telegraphed the Wuxing Court for an examination. The court sent a prosecutor to the scene yesterday with police officers. The examination found that the deceased had indeed died from injuries, and the Eighth Branch of the town escorted Yang Shi to Huzhou for legal proceedings.

Local News

Yesterday's Two Grand Banquets Hosted for Finance Minister Song Upon Return from Overseas

Twenty-Five Groups Hosted a Luncheon Banquet

Mayor Wu Also Held a Tea Party in the Evening

Song Ziwen, the Vice President of the Executive Yuan and Minister of Finance, arrived in Shanghai on the President Jefferson the day before yesterday. All sectors of the city, because Song has traveled far and wide for the country, organized a welcome back convention for Minister Song and hosted a luncheon banquet for Song at the City Chamber of Commerce yesterday at around 12:00 pm. More than 40 representatives from all walks of life attended, and leaders from all walks of life gave very cordial welcome speeches. Song also gave a speech, which was broadcasted by wireless radio. At 5:00 pm, Mayor Wu held a tea party at the City Government Garden at 1881 Xiafei Road to welcome Song. Details are described as follows:

Grand Banquets from All Sectors

Yesterday, the organizations participating in the welcome banquet for Mr. Song included 25 groups such as the Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce, the Shanghai General Labor Union, the Navigation Workers' Union, the Shanghai Fishermen's Association, the Shanghai Farmers' Association, the China Aviation Association, the Boy Scouts Council, the Chinese Ratepayers Association of the International Settlement, the Chinese Ratepayers Association of the French Concession, the Shanghai Educational Association, the Accountants' Association, the Local Autonomy Association, the Postal Workers' Union, the Money Trade Association, the Banking Workers' Union, the First Special District Citizens' Federation, the Second Special District Citizens' Federation, the Middle School Students' Federation, the University Students' Federation, the Middle School Teachers' Federation, the University Teachers' Federation, the National Postal Workers' Union, the International Problems Research Association, and the Pacific International Association. The chief host was Wang Xiaolai, Chairman of the Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce.

The venue was decorated at the gate of the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, fully adorned with colorful flowers, and a ceremonial arch was erected, inscribed with the words "Shanghai All Sectors Welcome Minister Song's Return to the Country Meeting." After entering the gate, national flags and colorful paper were hung straight to the hall. In the middle of the hall hung a horizontal banner with the large characters "Shanghai All Sectors Welcome Minister Song's Return to the Country Meeting," and above it was a horizontal plaque with the four large characters "Laboring for the Country." The four walls were covered with various slogans, such as "Welcome Minister Song to realize his grand economic plan after returning to the country," "Welcome Minister Song's efforts in economic construction," "Welcome Minister Song, who defends against foreign aggression and saves the country," "Welcome Minister Song, who develops China's industry," and so on. National flags of various countries were hung in the middle. A horizontal table was set up in the venue for Minister Song and the accompanying guests, and the rest were straight rows of seats for the guests.

Stringent Security As for the security of the venue, the Municipal Public Security Bureau specially dispatched a team of armed police officers to the venue for protection, and the 642nd Boy Scout Regiment maintained order. Armed patrol officers stood at the gate, prohibiting idlers from entering. The Public Concession Police Department also specially dispatched Chinese and Western detectives to protect the area outside the venue.

Accompanying Guests In addition to the representatives of the 25 organizations hosting the banquet who were sent to the venue to entertain, other guests invited to attend the banquet included Kong Xiangxi, President of the Central Bank; Bei Songsun, Manager of the Bank of China; Zou Lin, Vice Minister of Finance; Wu Tiecheng, Mayor of Shanghai; Yu Qiaqing, representative of the Chinese Ratepayers of the Public Concession; Zheng Hongnian, President of Jinan University; Du Yuesheng, representative of the Local Autonomy Association; Yang Hu, Director of the Security Department; Tang Haian, Superintendent of the Jianghai Customs; Xu Peihuang, Director of the Public Utilities Bureau; Wen Hongen, Director of the Public Security Bureau; Cai Zengji, Director of the Finance Bureau; Lin Kanghou, Hu Bijang, Ye Fuxiao, Yang Dunfu, Sun Jingxi, Xu Xinliu, and Xu Jichu, representatives of the banking industry; Pei Yunqing, representative of the money trade industry; Lu Wenshao, Chen Songyuan, Ye Jiaxing, Wang Hanliang, and Lao Jingxiu of the Municipal Chamber of Commerce; Lu Bohong, Manager of the China General Edison Company; Zhang Xiang, Chief of Staff of the Garrison Headquarters; Yuan Ludeng of the Shipping Association; Chen Chengzhizhi, Jiang Rujun, and Wu Yucang of the Aviation Association; Shen Junru of the Lawyers Association; Wen LantIng of the Food Industry Association; and Tao Baichuan of the Municipal Education Association, totaling hundreds of people. Mayor Wu Tiecheng left in advance. At about 1 p.m., Minister Song, accompanied by Wang Xiaolai and others, arrived at the venue and took their seats amidst the lively music and applause. Westerners in the venue used broadcasting radios to broadcast the event, and many Chinese and Western photographers took photos of Mr. Song.

Chairman's Speech Chairman Wang Xiaolai gave a welcome speech, saying, "When our association and others saw Minister Song off to the United States to attend the World Economic Conference, we once offered some suggestions, as the ancients did when they parted, thinking it would be helpful to support his profound insight. Time flies like an arrow, and in a blink of an eye, the conference closed. Our public has also completed the task, and the important position of agricultural minister should not be vacant for long, so he returned to the country with a flourish. This trip has made us feel that the international infighting is endless, and the so-called cooperation and coordination is still a kind of illusory ideal. Moreover, domestic border police and floods are coming one after another, making the rulers almost unable to have time to eat. We have been separated from you for several months, and as soon as we enter the country, we have not found any good news to comfort each other. This is something that all the people present should feel the same. Then, what is the meaning and feeling of today's grand meeting? We have to express it to Mr. Song and the guests present at this time. When our country was in the Qing Dynasty and Russia and Japan were fighting, there were many people who thought that China's weakness and the balance of power in the Far East were not easy to maintain. We should imitate the example of the Russian Emperor's appointment of foreign powers, and finally protect ourselves. We should send close and important ministers to travel around the world to change international views and connect international public opinion. Unfortunately, He Fei died early at that time, and no one among the Manchurian nobles could shoulder this important task. This proposal eventually fell through. The situation in which our country is today is a hundred times more difficult than in the Qing Dynasty. The reason is that Europe and the United States have many accidents and only want to protect themselves. The situation in the Far East has long lost its restraining effect. In this precarious situation, the national strength is not enough to defend itself. Therefore, struggling for survival still only seeks a way out in diplomacy. We read the history of Prussia and think that Prussia's unification of the whole of Germany, on the one hand, relied on Moltke's military strategy, and on the other hand, it also relied on Bismarck's use of diplomatic skills. At first, it allied with France to control Austria, and then it allied with Russia to frustrate France. All these situations are in the plan and need not be described in detail. Our country is far away in East Asia, and the situation does not have to be the same, but historical precedents are enough for people to refer to. Historically, diplomacy has been lost in dealing with things and lacking a consistent policy. Today, we must change this habit in order to protect ourselves. However, the decision of diplomatic policy must first be based on an accurate observation of the international situation. Therefore, it is not difficult to make a decision, but it is difficult to observe it correctly. Mr. Song took the opportunity to participate in the World Economic Conference, and his footprints have been all over the major countries in Europe, and he has been dealing with their important figures for several months. Therefore, this kind of diplomatic information cannot be collected by any capable minister. Although our country's diplomatic policy is determined by the Central Political Conference, the plan must be based on Mr. Song's information. If we compare it to sailing, we rely on you as the compass. Therefore, the fate of our country for the next few decades or hundreds of years is entrusted to the diplomatic policy after this, and the policy will not be confused in the trend, and it all depends on your good plan. Therefore, today our association held an unprecedented grand ceremony to welcome you back to the country, because this trip is entrusted by hundreds of millions of people, so the expectations are deep and sincere. In addition, the point of expectation is that our country's rural areas are bankrupt, and imports have exceeded about 300 million yuan in the first half of this year. The first place is still food, and the second place is still textiles. Domestic textile factories have reduced work for several months, but it has not helped the crisis, and even worse. Therefore, if our country wants to seek remedial measures, it must understand the international economic situation and implement the means of the US president's great reforms. Looking around the country, I am afraid that you are the only one who can do it. This is especially what our association wants to represent all sectors and express its expectations to you. The journey has just ended, and we are thinking about your hard work. We only hope that you will cherish your health for the country. I respectfully offer a toast to wish you good health."

Commemorative Silver Medal The commemorative silver medal presented by the Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce and other 25 organizations was written by Zhang Shizhao. After the welcome speeches, Mr. Song reported on the process of going abroad and gave a reply.

Mr. Song's reply Minister Song then stood up and gave a reply, saying, "Fellow compatriots, representatives, I am very grateful for your welcome at the dock yesterday and for your warm and grand banquet today. I am deeply ashamed. I originally planned to stay abroad for two months, but I extended it due to circumstances, so I have not met with you for four months. During my time in Europe and the United States, I discussed important issues with leaders of various countries, all of which are related to the practical cooperation between our country and various countries in economy. After reporting to the government, I will discuss it with you again. China's current economic decline and rural bankruptcy have indeed fallen into difficulties, but after observing from various countries, this state of depression is not unique to China, and all countries are like this. Therefore, during the journey in various countries, whether I was taking a train or eating, I saw unemployed people everywhere. Various countries have deeply felt the suffering of economic panic, so they believe that saving economic panic is an urgent task, and they have devoted their full efforts to cope with the difficult situation. As a result, there is a determination for major reforms, and capitalism has also changed due to the economic panic in various countries, such as the inheritance tax in the United States, which has been increased from 60% to 84% by the government. This is one example. In the financial aspect, the monetary system was resolutely reformed and the gold standard was abandoned. This should not have been the case in the United States, because it is a country with more exports and a creditor country to various countries. However, because various countries are in the frenzy of economic panic, President Roosevelt resolutely implemented it because his purpose was to raise prices. However, he has a certain method and a certain step in implementing this matter. Private individuals must not arbitrarily interfere in any undertaking, and the government implements the principle of intervention. Capitalists are not allowed to oppress workers, and workers are not allowed to strike without reason. Even in emerging countries such as Russia, Italy, and Germany, regardless of their political fascism or communism, their purpose is to seek the common welfare of society and the country. Only in this way can they sacrifice their own rights. Our country has strong enemies pressing down from abroad, communist disturbances within, and economic panic has reached its extreme. In the future, we must unite and unite to have the possibility of development and the hope of becoming strong. Taking the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company as an example, in the era of commercial management, due to various malpractices, the business was poor, and the status quo failed, and the sovereignty was completely invaded by foreigners. Now that it has been taken back under state management, the directors and managers are still hired by merchants to preside over. Only in this way can the government and the people cooperate. In the past year, the business situation has greatly improved compared to before. Recently, from the British Boxer Indemnity, loans have been borrowed, and seven new ships have been ordered from the United Kingdom to develop our country's shipping industry. The result of my contact with various countries this time is that all countries can help our country. Therefore, if the domestic commercial, industrial, and financial sectors can implement the principle of unity and cooperate in both production and sales, China, although poor, will surely be able to achieve great things. The reason is that there are millions of unemployed workers in various countries, and there is a surplus of production. It is not a problem that they can help me. However, under this situation in China, whether it can succeed still requires China to have a sound organization and the people can be united. If there is a sound model area, and gradually extend to various places, then it will be sound. The most feared thing for foreigners investing in our country is that there are often problems in our country, and the people cannot be united. Therefore, in the face of internal and external troubles, the only way is to jointly seek unity. If we can unite, then industry will be revitalized, and if industry is revitalized, then politics and diplomacy will have hope. Therefore, after receiving your grand banquet today, I dare to offer these points to you."

Direct Train between Shanghai and Peiping Starts Tomorrow

丨The Shanghai-Nanking Line Will Also Revise the Train Schedule at the Same Time丨

The direct train between Shanghai and Peiping, which has been in preparation for a long time, has now been decided to start tomorrow, and the Shanghai-Nanking Line will also revise the train schedule at the same time, adding a Zhenjiang-Shanghai mixed passenger train. The newly revised train times for the Shanghai-Peiping and Shanghai-Nanking lines are as follows:

Direct Train between Shanghai and Peiping Starts

Train Announcement

The announcement of the direct train between Shanghai and Peiping says: "Starting from September 1st, this railway will have one express train running between Shanghai and Peiping every day. Before the ferry is open, it will be temporarily transported by the Chengping Ferry to shorten the travel time. The travel time between Shanghai and Peiping is only 43 hours and 48 minutes. The equipment of the improved vehicles, all the vehicles attached to the Shanghai-Peiping through train are luxurious new steel cars. The vehicles of other express trains are clean and complete, safe, fast and comfortable. Special announcement."
