Funeral Situation: The funeral was held at 2 p.m. yesterday. The family members paid tribute, followed by the groups and guests. The family members replied to the groups and guests, and finally moved the coffin to the funeral home, and the ceremony was concluded. On the same day, the Central Party Department, the Central Propaganda Committee, representatives of the Municipal Party Department, Mayor Wu, Director Yang of the Security Office, Director Wen of the Public Security Bureau, and more than 400 guests from all walks of life arrived.

A New Contribution from the World Industry Society

The World Industry Society of the Jiande Lane, at the intersection of Gordon Road and Connaught Road in this city, manufactures various celluloid floral pedestals, billiard balls, square, round, and other types of tabletop mirrors, unique cigarette cases, soap dishes, and modern powder boxes. The factory is grand in scale, perfectly equipped, and uses the latest machines and scientific manufacturing techniques, so its products are excellent and its prices are low. It is truly a rising star among domestic celluloid factories. Recently, it has added new machines and already has a large batch of products, with those coming to order them being extremely enthusiastic.

Soldier Wei Guobin Disappears

The Shanghai Garrison Headquarters, based on a report from Peng Shanhou, the battalion commander of the 1st Battalion of the Military Police, stated that Wei Guobin, a private first class in the 3rd Machine Gun Company of this regiment, had reported that his family lived in Zhabei, Shanghai. Now, someone had come to the company to say that his younger brother was critically ill and begged to be allowed to take leave to visit him. On the 20th of this month, he was granted one day of personal leave and ordered to go in plain clothes. By the morning of the 21st, he had not returned to the company. 2nd Lieutenant Yu Songsheng and Sergeant Xu Caiming were sent to inquire at his home. Only then did they learn that his younger brother had already died. According to his father, his younger son had an argument last night over money problems and had gone out and not returned. On the same day, they received a letter from the soldier, stating that his younger brother had died, that he had no money for the funeral, that his grandmother was critically ill and he could not care for her, and that he was filled with despair about the future and only wished to die. The soldier had boarded the Zhengtai steamship and decided to go to the Wusongkou to drown himself in the river. However, inquiries with the shipping company revealed that there was no such incident. Military and police authorities are currently searching in separate directions.

Yu Huizhao, Former Magistrate of Jinjiang County, Fujian, Arrested in Shanghai for Embezzling Funds During His Tenure

Will Be Escorted Back to Fujian to Be Prosecuted According to Law

The Fujian Department of Finance stated that Yu Huizhao (from Jiangxi), the former magistrate of Jinjiang County in the province, embezzled public funds during his tenure, including over ten thousand in funds for the airfield and road construction, and had not reported them to higher authorities. After the case was discovered, the provincial government issued an arrest warrant. Yu went into hiding and came to Shanghai a month ago. Shen Wenda, a detective from the Public Security Bureau, discovered his whereabouts and urgently reported to Captain Lu. Detective Jiao Baojun and Zhu Fusheng were dispatched, together with detectives from the French Concession's Lujiawan Police Station, all in disguise, to No. 1 Cishou South Lane on Avenue Joffre. Detective Shen, disguised as a tea waiter, claimed to be sent by a certain Master Shi from a certain room at the Greater China Hotel, asking Magistrate Yu to come for a talk. He was received by a Mr. Xu, who believed it to be true and replied that Yu was currently residing at No. 10 Yongqing Lane on Rue Béthune and could be reached directly. Shen and the others then went to the address, where they found Yu Huizhao reading a newspaper in the parlor. They immediately arrested him and took him into custody. Later, Yu claimed to be ill and requested bail, and offered to immediately send someone to Fujian to handle the procedures from his tenure, but the request was denied. It is now known that the Fujian Department of Finance has commissioned Mo Wenhui to bring a document to Shanghai to escort him back. It is said that Director Wen has approved, so Mo is scheduled to take Yu on the Huaan steamer this week to Fuzhou to be prosecuted according to law.

Wife Urges Husband to Return Home from a Mahjong Game at a Friend's House, Is Humiliated, and Commits Suicide by Poisoning

Zhou Xue, a woman from Ningbo, 22 years old, lived at No. 130, Taian Lane, Tiantong Road. Her husband, Zhou Shoukang, used to work in the stock exchange, but is now unemployed at home. One morning around 1:00 AM, Zhou was playing mahjong at a friend's house for fun. Because her husband had not returned late at night, Ms. Zhou went to the place to urge her husband to return home with her. Unexpectedly, Zhou not only refused to listen but also humiliated and scolded his wife. Unable to do anything, Ms. Zhou returned home alone. After much thought, she was filled with resentment and despair and conceived a desire to end her life. She secretly swallowed opium and committed suicide. Her husband noticed and sent her to Guangren Hospital for treatment, but it was ineffective, and she soon died. The hospital reported it to the police station, which ordered detectives to investigate. The body was taken to the Phylun Road morgue for examination. Yesterday morning, Guo Wei, a prosecutor from the First Special District Court, arrived at the morgue to conduct an examination and determined that the cause of death was suicide. According to Zhou Shoukang, the husband of the deceased, he was playing mahjong at a friend's house that day and the game was not yet over. His wife suddenly came and ordered him to return home. Because he was concerned about his reputation in front of his friends at that time, he scolded her slightly. He did not expect her to commit suicide after returning home. After hearing his statement, Guo concluded that the deceased, Zhou Xue, died of opium poisoning before her death. The body was released to her husband, Zhou Shoukang, to be placed in a coffin for burial after he signed a guarantee.

Liuhe Will Rebuild the New and Old Floating Bridges

First Committee Meeting Held Yesterday

The new and old floating bridges in Liuhe were previously damaged in the war and have suffered from disrepair over the years. Many of the bridge timbers are broken, making it very dangerous for pedestrians. Therefore, the local gentry and merchants organized a Bridge Construction Committee to find ways to rebuild them. The first committee meeting was held yesterday, attended by more than twenty people including Xiang Ganbo, Lu Renxi, Zhong Yinsheng, Qian Baichuan, Mei Youzhi, Huang Songsheng, Zhu Kaichou, and Wu Zhongyi. Mao Lupu was elected as chairman. After the formalities were completed, the chairman reported the purpose of the meeting. Then, Zhu Kaichou reported that the construction of the old floating bridge is planned to use reinforced concrete, costing about 18,000 silver dollars. The new floating bridge will cost about 12,000 silver dollars. Except for the negotiations with various parties, there are already about seven or eight thousand silver dollars in sight, but there is still a significant shortage. He hopes that the gentlemen present will work hard to solicit donations so that it can be completed soon. Next, Xiang Huaqing said that he owned a residence located on the west side of the North Stone Bridge in Liuhe Town, and after selling it, he would use the entire amount to fund the bridge construction. Then, the following proposals were discussed: (1) Zhu Kaichou proposed that the construction of the two bridges was originally planned to be carried out simultaneously, but due to economic constraints, the old floating bridge should be rebuilt first, and the old materials removed from the old floating bridge should be temporarily repaired and used for the new floating bridge to save money. The resolution was passed. (2) Zhang Lunqing proposed that because it is not easy to raise funds, a bridge should be built in a central location between the two bridges. The resolution involved changing the transportation plan, and the opinions of the majority of the local people should be sought, and a proposal should be submitted to the county government. (3) Zhu Kaichou proposed that Lu Renxi be appointed as the engineer for the reconstruction of the two bridges. The resolution was passed. (4) Zhu Kaichou proposed that the committee members personally send the donation registers to the absent committee members. It was resolved to appoint Song Kaichou and Huang Songsheng as representatives to personally send the donation registers. (5) The chairman proposed that the Second District Office should submit the bridge construction plan to the county for record. The proposal was passed. Finally, Zhang Lunqing, Xiang Huaqing, Fu Yongyan, Wang Puhuan, Zhong Yinsheng, and Zhu Kaichou were appointed as economic committee members, and Lu Renxi, Huang Songsheng, Wu Zhongyi, Zhu Qizhan, and Huang Qiusheng were appointed as engineering committee members, and the meeting adjourned.

Zhou Xiuying is Missing; A Reward of One Hundred Dollars Will Be Given to Anyone Who Can Find the Child

Zhou Xiuying, a four-year-old girl with the surname Zhou, residing at No. 37 Tingyuan Lane, Pingwang Street, Wuma Road, Public Concession, suddenly went missing while playing in the neighborhood around 10:00 AM the day before yesterday. In addition to the girl's mother reporting to the relevant police station and requesting them to investigate the girl's whereabouts, they have also printed leaflets with the girl's clothes and appearance at the time of her disappearance, and distributed rewards. Lu Ganchen Appointed as General Secretary of the YMCA

Mr. Lu Ganchen, who has recently returned from studying in Europe, has been appointed as the General Secretary of the Shanghai YMCA by the Board of Directors, and will officially take office on September 1. Mr. Lu is a native of Wuxing, Zhejiang, and is 35 years old. After graduating from Soochow University, he founded the Suzhou YMCA. He then studied at Vanderbilt University and Yale University in the United States, researching social politics and obtaining a master's degree. After returning to China, he served as the secretary of the National YMCA Association, and was later transferred to the position of director of the City Association Group. He has made many contributions to various City Associations. Last year, he was invited by the University of Oxford in England to study in England and to investigate the social conditions of various European countries. He returned to China last month and accepted the invitation from the Shanghai YMCA.

Completion of the Jinrong Bridge in Caohejing

Traffic Ceremony to Be Held on September 1

A stone bridge in the east market of Caohejing Town, Shanghai, was inconvenient for vehicles due to its height and narrowness. Therefore, a road was built on the south side of the bridge, connecting Caoxi Road to the east and Bijiao Road to the west, reaching the Huang Family Garden. It was a major east-west thoroughfare. This spring, due to the opening of a new port and dredging of the north and south rivers, the original stone bridge was demolished, and the roadbed that had been used to fill the road was also dredged due to the waterway. It was necessary to build another bridge to facilitate transportation and benefit navigation. However, the river surface was wide, requiring a large amount of money. The municipal government was unable to plan for it for a time due to financial constraints. Later, Mr. Huang Jinrong independently donated 6,500 silver dollars. The Bureau of Public Works contracted Qian Yongji to build a reinforced concrete bridge. Construction has been underway for three months and all projects are now complete. A traffic ceremony will be held on September 1, and it will be named Jinrong Bridge.

Publishing World

Outline of Pre-Qin Literature Published: The Outline of Pre-Qin Literature, compiled by Yang Yin Shen, is the first volume of the Outline of Chinese Literature. The entire book contains 160,000 words, with three sections and twelve chapters. It covers everything about Pre-Qin literature, from ancient times to the Qin Dynasty, providing comprehensive and detailed descriptions. In particular, the sections on poetry and Chu Ci are the most vivid. The compiler based it on his daily research and can provide precise interpretations of the literary works of each era, without following the old patterns of his predecessors. For works with profound and obscure texts, he can use his moving writing style to provide very clear explanations. Furthermore, the entire book includes many beautiful illustrations, which are rare outside. At the end of the book, there is also a table of dates, an index, and a bibliography, which are especially convenient for checking and reference. It is truly the best book for studying Chinese literature. It is now published and available in paperback for eight dimes and hardcover for one dollar and two dimes. Published by Huatong Bookstore, 4th Road, Shanghai.

Education News

Important News

Annual Conference of the China Library Association

Request that Schools and Public Libraries Seek Independent Funding

Next Annual Conference to Be Held in Wuchang, Hangzhou, or Guangzhou

(Special Dispatch from Beiping) The Second Annual Conference of the China Library Association opened on the 28th in the auditorium of Tsinghua University in the suburbs of Beiping. Party, government, and education officials all attended the conference. The annual conference ceremony was held at 9:00 AM and adjourned at 11:10 AM. Group meetings of the administrative group were held from 2:00 PM to 5:00 PM. On the 29th (the second day), the funding group meeting was originally scheduled to be held at the Biology Museum at 8:00 AM, but due to the rain, the committee members living in the city were unable to arrive in time, and the meeting was changed to 2:00 PM in the afternoon. However, the meeting for the discussion of association affairs was still held at 10:00 AM in the morning, and the location was changed to the Third Academy. The Second Annual Conference of the China Library Association is a general gathering of library experts from all over the country and has made a great contribution to education and culture. The reporter made a special trip of more than twenty li for several days to attend the conference at Tsinghua University. The reporter received the warm reception of the chairmen of the association, Yuan Tongli, Wang Wenshan, and Shen Zurong, as well as the members of the reception group. The details of the association are recorded as follows.

Grand Opening Ceremony

At 9:00 AM on the 28th, the association held a general meeting at Tsinghua University. The venue was set up in the Tsinghua University auditorium. The chairmen of the association, Yuan Tongli, Wang Wenshan, and Shen Zurong, and the guests Yuan Liang, Zhao Shuyong, and Fan Jichang, etc., were on the stage. The first row below the stage was the reporter's seat, and the second row was also the reporter's seat, but there were no reporters present. The third row was the seat for female members, including Ms. Lu Xiaoxin, and the rows after that were for the members' seats. After the meeting began, the Tsinghua Military Band played music and performed the formalities. The chairmen of the association jointly elected Yuan Tongli, the deputy director of the Beiping Library, to deliver the opening speech.

Chairman's Speech: Chairman Yuan briefly stated that today, the Second Annual Conference of the China Library Association is held at Tsinghua University. It is a great honor to have the party, government, and education officials and guests attend the conference. The China Library Association was established in June 1925, and the first annual conference was held in Nanjing in January 1929. This year's second annual conference is held in Beiping. It is not easy to gather librarians from all over the country in one hall. There are three difficulties: (1) The association's funds are insufficient. (2) Due to the situation, the scheduled dates often have to be postponed. (3) There are many proposals for the annual conference, and it takes a long time to implement them. The scope of discussion for this annual conference is limited to funding and public education, which has already been explained in the declaration of the Second Annual Conference. Now, I would like to add a few points: (1) In terms of architecture, the libraries of Tsinghua University, the National Beiping Library, the Guangzhou City Library, and the Zhejiang Provincial Library in Hangzhou all have magnificent and luxurious buildings. (2) In terms of content, the purchase of books by Beiping City has an annual budget of more than 500,000, totaling more than 2 million in four years. Book purchases are divided into labor and cooperation, with mutual contact. (3) In terms of public education, public education has developed in the past four years, and the number of public libraries has increased. The number of public libraries in Jiangsu and Zhejiang has increased, and public libraries in Hebei and Shandong have also gradually been added due to the impact of the popularization of public education. There has been progress in both quality and quantity. The only point of dissatisfaction is funding. The funding situation varies from place to place, and the two Guangs cannot develop evenly. Libraries in the interior are lagging behind. The mission of the association is to enable libraries across the country to develop simultaneously and to provide scholars in the interior with research opportunities. The funding of libraries is beyond the capacity of librarians and requires the assistance of local authorities. In recent years, China's construction projects have been concentrated in cities, and the bourgeoisie has entered the cities, resulting in a deformed development. This is not a good phenomenon. In the future, we will concentrate the strength of the whole country and proceed towards the countryside to ensure that the people have the opportunity to read books and develop public libraries.

Huang Fu's Opinion: Huang Fu delivered a speech on behalf of Zhao Shuyong, briefly stating that he was very honored to participate in the grand meeting on behalf of Chairman Huang. China is originally the oldest country in terms of culture and academics. The China Library Association focuses on the library, an important part of culture and academics. The future restoration of Chinese culture depends entirely on the library community. The Chinese have the following concepts about books: (1) Pay attention to Song editions. Some people will not read anything other than Song editions. (2) Collation and printing. Judge the quality of the published editions. (3) Collectors specialize in collecting ancient books. Today's libraries pay attention to public education. Popular books are also collected, and printing books is also very important. The Ministry of Education printed a shadow copy of the Siku Quanshu, and library experts contributed their opinions. At present, only a few people have this view. I hope that in the future, people across the country will pay attention to this.

Guest Speeches: (1) Pang Jingtang, representative of the Municipal Party Committee, delivered a speech with the following main points: (1) Villagers have no opportunity to seek knowledge and cannot even maintain their lives. (2) Relics other than the Siku Quanshu, national ideology, Qing documents, and the history of aggression in the last three hundred years should all be paid attention to. (2) Beiping Mayor Yuan Liang delivered a speech: (1) Library science is a specialized field, and this subject should be established in universities to promote culture. (2) In 1930, there were more than 2,900 libraries nationwide. This year, the number has doubled. (3) He hopes for two points: (a) To increase the effectiveness of library services; (b) To expand the library itself. (3) Tsinghua President Mei Yiqi delivered a speech: (1) Welcome the members of the China Library Association to hold a meeting at our school. (2) Report on the situation of the Tsinghua University Library. (3) Ask the members of the association for guidance. (4) Peking University President Jiang Menglin delivered a speech on behalf of Fan Jichang: (1) Various undertakings in China want to be done but have not been completed, but libraries have made great progress. (2) The equipment of libraries in various schools is incomplete. I hope that the association will support the research of teachers and students in various schools. (5) Li Shizeng, Director of the Beiping Research Institute, delivered a speech on behalf of Li Shengzhang: (1) The process of the establishment of the International Library. (2) The purpose of the International Library is to communicate Chinese and Western cultures. (3) The situation of cultural exchange between China and other countries.

Member's Reply: Liu Guojun was elected by the members to deliver a reply, briefly stating that he was grateful to the party, government, education officials, and guests for their instruction at the opening of the Second Annual Conference of the China Library Association. He expressed his gratitude on behalf of all the members. Eight years ago, the association was established in Beiping with the guidance of the government. Eight years later, the meeting was held again in Beiping and guidance was received again. It is a great honor and allows the members to visit the unscheduled scenery. The members will always remember the instructions of the speakers. Libraries promote culture, and Chinese culture will develop simultaneously. We will work harder for the library cause. What the Chinese nation invented: (1) Papermaking. It was invented during the Eastern Han Dynasty. The West had paper more than a thousand years later. (2) Printing. China invented printing in the second half of the Han Dynasty. The West was five hundred years later than China. What is China's current position? Can we bear this cultural responsibility and make the world's culture uplifted by China in the future? Without papermaking and printing, there would be no libraries. Finally, Li Wenqi, a member of the preparatory committee, reported on the arrangements for the group meetings. The meeting adjourned at 11:00 AM.

Resolutions of the Administrative Group

First, at 2:00 PM in the afternoon, the Library Administrative Group meeting was held in the Tsinghua Biology Museum. More than sixty committee members, including Yuan Tongli, Hong Youfeng, Feng Chen Zuyi, and Yao Jinzhong, attended. Yuan Tongli presided over the meeting and passed the following resolutions: (1) It is recommended that the provincial library should be the highest administrative executive agency of the provincial library and protect its administrative and administrative financial independence. The resolution was to appoint representatives from the libraries of Zhejiang, Jiangxi, Anhui, and Tianjin, and the original proposer to revise it and submit it to the next meeting. (2) Consider opening school libraries to integrate school books with society and subsidize adult education. The resolution was that the China Library Association should send a letter to the library of each school to consider opening it to the public for reading outside the school. (3) The Association should reward those who are enthusiastic and hardworking in the library cause. The resolution was to hand it over to the Executive Committee of the Association for handling. (4) Examine and approve the library administrator to promote the progress of the library cause. The resolution was to send it to the Library Education Group for combined discussion. (5) The staff members of various libraries in the country can exchange travel expenses and observation fees. The resolution was to pass it according to the original plan. (6) Libraries should also expand publicity methods to seek business development. Resolution: The first item of the original proposal, "Each library should specify an item for publicity expenses in its budget," was canceled, and the following were changed to one, two, three, and four in order. The last item was changed to "Each year, a national library movement week will be held on a specified date." (7) Please order the public libraries of each province, city, and county to set up a circulating book department. The resolution was that the association would again recommend that the public libraries of each province, city, and county set up a circulating department. The meeting adjourned at 5:00 PM.

Meeting Resolutions

On the second day (the 29th), the meeting of the council was held at 10:00 AM in the Third Hall of Tsinghua University. Over two hundred members attended, chaired by Dai Zhiqian, with Yuan Tongli acting as secretary. First, the chairman reported that the executive department of the association must compile a report annually to notify all members. As usual, the report is published in the first issue of each volume of the association journal. The annual report has already been published in the first issue of Volume 9. Members are requested to examine it themselves. Today's discussion will focus on how the association should develop. Based on personal experience, there are four reasons why the association has not been able to develop in recent years: (1) insufficient funding; (2) inability to hire full-time staff to take charge; (3) members are mostly serving in various libraries, making it difficult to concentrate on assisting the association, and executive committee members are scattered in different locations, making it difficult to convene meetings, rendering the committee virtually non-existent; (4) the publication of journals is often delayed due to members' lack of enthusiasm in submitting articles. It is proposed to use these four reasons for the lack of development as the focus of today's discussion, discussing them item by item. Next, the following resolutions were passed: (1) Resolution on the association's endowment fund: Fundraising methods include: (a) the association's institutional members and individual members will donate funds based on their income, according to the principle of proportion; (b) establish a fundraising committee, inviting enthusiastic library professionals from all walks of life to join as members; (c) send letters to central and local administrative agencies for subsidies; (d) after a certain amount has been raised, request subsidies from the Sino-British and Sino-American Foundations; (e) the association will establish an endowment fund management committee to be solely responsible for endowment fund management; (f) donations will be published in the association's journal and major newspapers in Shanghai and elsewhere; (g) detailed rules for the management committee will be determined separately. (2) Resolution on the location of the next annual meeting: Choose one of Wuchang, Hangzhou, and Guangzhou. (3) Resolution on the association immediately organizing a library weekly or shortening the publication period of the association journal to promote library services and disseminate library news: Resolved, to be handled by the editorial department taking into consideration the actual situation. (3) Resolution on stipulating that the association's office staff should be full-time positions to increase the efficiency of association affairs: Resolved, to be handled by the executive committee at its discretion. (4) Resolution on the association establishing a library personnel registration and referral department: Resolved, to be handled by the executive committee. The meeting adjourned at 12:30 PM.

Annual Meeting of the Chinese Institute of Engineers

Detailed Account of the Opening Day

(Central News Agency, Hankou, 29th) The third annual meeting of the Chinese Institute of Engineers opened at 10:00 AM on the 29th at Wuhan University on Luojia Mountain in Wuchang. More than two hundred members from various places, including Wu Chengluo, Ling Hongxun, and Hu Shuhua, attended, as well as Zhang Qun representing the Director of Construction, Li Fanyi, the Provincial and Municipal Party Committees, the Mayor of Hankou, Wu Guozhen, and dozens of representatives and guests from various organizations. After Chairman Shao Yizhou reported on the significance of holding the Wuhan Annual Meeting, Secretary-General Qiu Xieyun delivered a speech on behalf of President Yan Deqing. Next, Vice President Chen Zhengyu of the Wuhan Branch gave a welcome speech. Finally, the guests delivered speeches successively. Yang Zifu and Yang Xingqin of the Provincial and Municipal Party Committees delivered speeches, all hoping that the members would pay attention to preventing floods and developing transportation. Li Fanyi delivered a speech, hoping to establish their own reputation and contribute what they have learned to the country and the nation. The chairman gave a concluding speech, and the meeting adjourned at noon. At 1:00 PM, Wu Chengluo lectured on industrial standards at the College of Science. At 2:00 PM, after the council meeting at the College of Science, Chairman Zhang Yanxiang, in addition to Secretary-General Qiu Xieyun of the General Assembly reporting on association affairs and Accountant Zhang Xiaoji reporting on the financial situation, decided that the next annual meeting would be held in Guangzhou (if there are factual difficulties, Jinan may be the second choice for the annual meeting location, to be decided temporarily by the executive department). It was also decided that the group membership fee would be reduced to twenty yuan per year in order to achieve universality. The Election Committee reported the names of the next session of officers elected by members using communication methods, including President and Vice President Sa Fujun and Huang Boqiao, respectively. One-third of the directors were re-elected, and Ling Hongxun, Zhi Bingyuan, Zhang Yanxiang, Zeng Yangfu, and Hu Boyuan received the most votes. Mo Heng and Zhou Ren were fund supervisors. Shao Yizhou, Zhang Yanxiang, Chen Zhengyu, Miao Sizhao, and Fang Boquan were elected as members of the next Election Committee. The meeting adjourned at 5:00 PM. The members then took cars to tour the scenery near Wuhan University and then went to Baobing Hall for a banquet hosted by Huazhong University, Central China University, and Jingcheng Electric Light Company. During the banquet, Chen Shizhi delivered a welcome speech, and the members elected Chen Zhengyu to respond. The meeting ended at 8:00 PM in a joyous atmosphere. The conference held a paper session on the morning of the 30th and continued to discuss proposals.

Departing for Chengdu, Public Lectures on Scientific Development

Relief Measures for the Qualifications of Graduates from Specialized Schools and Above Before Registration

The Ministry of Education issued an order to private specialized schools and above, stating that the Ministry had already stipulated methods for the retroactive recognition of the qualifications of graduates from private specialized schools and above before registration in Bulletins Nos. 8 and 9 of the 19th year. The main restriction was that "the level of the school at the time of graduation is equal to the level of the school at the time of registration." Since implementation, the reports from various schools have indicated that many do not meet the original standards. In order to facilitate processing, the Ministry has specifically announced the handling standards in detail. For those who do not obtain retroactive recognition according to the standards, two qualification examination trials will be added for relief. The methods are as follows: (1) Schools that were recognized by the former Beijing Ministry of Education before registration, the qualifications of graduates during the period of interruption of recognition are permitted to be retroactively recognized. (2) Schools that were not recognized by the former Beijing Ministry of Education before registration, if the management is indeed successful and there are none of the various situations listed in Item 4, the qualifications of their graduates before registration are permitted to be retroactively recognized. (3) Schools that were recognized by the former Beijing Ministry of Education before registration, the qualifications of graduates before the recognition are still not retroactively recognized. (4) Schools that were not recognized by the former Beijing Ministry of Education before registration, if any of the following situations occur, the qualifications of their graduates before registration should not be retroactively recognized: (A) those provisionally approved for registration; (B) those ordered to improve at the time of registration; (C) those found to be poorly managed and ordered to improve after registration; (D) those who fail to submit new student admission documents in accordance with regulations after registration, or more than 30% of the new student admission qualifications do not meet the regulations, or there are repeated cases of forgery or impersonation of diplomas. (5) If any school has graduates who meet the provisions of Items 1 or 2, when requesting retroactive recognition of qualifications, the school should obtain the following documents and submit them to the Ministry for approval of retroactive recognition, which will be filed for future reference and returned with a stamp: (A) Academic transcripts detailing the names of each course taken in each semester, the number of class hours per week, the grades, the names of the teachers in charge, and their signatures and seals (if the teacher has passed away, the head of the department or the current president of the college when the student graduated is responsible for certifying, signing, and sealing the transcript) to be submitted to the Ministry for filing. If the student transferred from another specialized school or above, a copy of the original school's academic transcript must be added. A recent 2.5-inch half-length photo must be affixed to the academic transcript. (B) The graduation certificate from the secondary school before admission. If the student transferred from another specialized school or above, a transfer certificate from the original school must also be added, which will be verified and returned. (C) The graduation certificate will be verified and returned with the Ministry's seal after approval for retroactive recognition. A 2.5-inch half-length photo, the same as the one on the academic transcript, must be affixed to the certificate. (6) Graduates whose qualifications are not retroactively recognized according to the above standards may submit a request to the Ministry through the original school to take the qualification examination for graduates from private specialized schools and above before registration. The methods are as follows: (A) Submit the documents required for requesting retroactive recognition of qualifications in accordance with Item 5 through the original school to the Ministry and apply to take the examination. Those who are approved will be registered. (B) The qualification examination will be held by the Ministry on a regular basis, and the Ministry will publish a notice in the newspaper one month before the examination for the approved registered students. (C) The examination subjects are divided into general and specialized categories. The general subjects are Chinese Language and Party Principles (Three Principles of the People). There will be five to eight specialized subjects, which will also be notified one month before the examination. (D) The graduation qualifications of graduates who pass the qualification examination will be recognized. (E) Each student is limited to two qualification examinations. In addition to the distribution to various departments, this order is issued to be followed. This order.

Shandong to Participate in the National Games with Track and Field All-Around

Decision Not to Send Swimming and Ball Teams

丨丨North China Ball Games Cannot Expand Facilities丨丨

(Jinan Correspondence) This province originally planned to participate in this year's National Games by selecting all-around track and field athletes for both men and women, as well as representative teams for various ball games, and had also built a swimming pool to prepare to send swimming athletes. Unexpectedly, the Yellow River caused damage, and western Shandong has become a flooded country. The provincial government and local disaster relief are overwhelmed, and the preliminary selection for the National Games has been reduced in scope. After continuous consultations between the Department of Education and the competition director of the National Games preliminary selection preparatory committee, Shang Shumei, it has been decided that the National Games preliminary selection meeting will only be held for three days from September 15th to 17th to select all-around track and field athletes for both men and women. Ball teams will not be selected. Schools with swimming competitions can also compete, but athletes will not be sent.

Also, this year's winter vacation, the North China Football and Basketball Games, has been decided to be held in Jinan. The North China Sports Federation had previously telegraphed to request proper facilities, so the sports field prepared to build a gym with tens of thousands of yuan last month, and had requested drawings from Tsinghua University, and repaired the three-sided stands of the ball field, but recently it has also been suspended due to the flood. Shang Shumei, the director of the sports field, will go to Beijing in the next few days to attend the North China Sports Federation. The Department of Education is preparing an official letter to be entrusted to Shang to take with him, which mainly states that if the football and basketball games this year are held in Shandong, they are still very welcome, but this province has suffered a severe flood and cannot make expanded and perfect facilities.

Publication of "Methods for Implementing Health Education" Edited by Wang Geng

Individual ill-health inevitably leads to unemployment, non-productivity, suffering, and poverty. National ill-health inevitably leads to national spirit decline, national weakness, societal corruption, and frequent foreign invasions. Recognizing this, the central government has been actively promoting health education for the populace in recent days. However, in this nascent stage, there are no specialized books on this subject within the country, leaving those engaged in general health education without a reference. This is deeply regrettable. Now, the Qinfen Bookstore at 392 Rue du Père Robert (opposite the National Sports Advancement Association) in the French Concession of Shanghai has engaged Mr. Wang Geng, Director of Physical Education at the Jiangsu Provincial Educational Institute, to edit "Methods for Implementing Health Education." The book is now published. Mr. Wang has been involved in health education for many years and is rich in both knowledge and experience. The content of this work is comprehensive, and the evidence presented is accurate. It can be considered his masterpiece. Furthermore, it has been implemented for many years in the Wuxi Experimental Zone and is highly practical. The entire book is divided into two parts, upper and lower, with four chapters in the upper part and six chapters in the lower part, each chapter further divided into sections. Chapter 1, "The Physiological Basis of Healthy Habits," includes ten sections on food, large muscle exercise, sleep, air and ventilation, excretion, and more. Chapter 2, "Basic Knowledge of Disease Prevention," includes seven sections on the sources of disease and microorganisms, opportunities for bacteria to enter the human body, what happens after bacteria enter the human body, and the phenomena of infectious diseases. Chapter 3, "Preventive Medical Health," Section 1 covers diseases that can be completely prevented or treated with certainty, including eleven points on diphtheria, smallpox, cholera, dysentery, hookworm disease, etc. Section 2 covers diseases that can be prevented by isolating patients or carriers, including twelve points on tuberculosis, pneumonia, whooping cough, measles, etc. Section 3 covers diseases that can be prevented by improving lifestyle habits, including six points on diabetes, gout, stroke, etc. Section 4 covers diseases that can be prevented by popularizing public health education, including eleven points on malnutrition, neurasthenia, indigestion, etc. Chapter 4, "Publicity for Public Health Undertakings," includes four points on who our target audience for publicity is, etc. The lower part covers public health guidance. Chapter 1, "Public Health and Vital Statistics," includes seven points on infant mortality, accidental deaths, population statistics, disease statistics, etc. Chapter 2, "The Administrative System of Public Health," includes seven sections on a brief description of the public health administrative organization, etc. Chapter 3 includes six sections on a brief description of food types and methods for food identification, etc. Chapter 4, "Three Major Issues in Public Health," includes three sections on the disposal of water, feces, and waste, etc. Chapter 5 includes five sections on clothing, housing, bathing, hairdressing, and soil, etc. Chapter 6, "The Formulation of Health Regulations," includes ten sections on the training of old-style midwives, cleaning roads, banning toilets, and restaurants, etc. The entire work spans over 100,000 words and includes dozens of accurate charts and diagrams. It is truly a must-read for those involved in public education centers and public education personnel. The entire book is in one volume, beautifully bound, and priced at $1.40. A special discount of 10% is offered. Mail orders with registered postage cost $0.14. It is also available at the bookstore's sales department at 554 Sima Road, British Concession, Shanghai.

Diary of the Wimbledon World Tennis Championships (8)

Special Correspondent in London, Yizhi

July 5th (Wednesday), continued from yesterday

Although the first two sets were close, Crawford controlled the situation. There were more errors in this match than in the previous one. For example, in the first set, Sato and Crawford were tied 2-2. Crawford missed four easy volleys. Sato won the opponent's serve to lead 4-3. Crawford then took the lead at 5-3 through two net cords and a double fault from Sato due to bad luck, winning the set 6-3. In the second set, after 3-3, Sato improved, but Crawford still won 6-4. Sato's luck was particularly bad. At 4-5, he only needed two points to make it 5-5 but touched the net twice.

Crawford took the opportunity to advance. Some of his errors were inexcusable. Sato was much improved in the third set, winning five games in a row. Crawford's attempts to approach the net were all passed. Crawford was down 0-30 on his serve, and it seemed Sato would win the set easily, but Crawford took six and seven games. Then, Crawford's service game was full of countless errors, not winning a single point.

In the first five games of the fourth set, the server lost each time. The match gradually improved, with good and bad shots from both sides. At 4-4, Sato served, and the battle intensified. They went back and forth. Sato double-faulted, giving Crawford a point lead but then touched the net and followed with a shot out. Sato took the lead again, but he sent one of his easiest backhand smashes into the net. Sato looked disappointed, while Crawford shouted in extreme horror. Crawford then hit a shot to the baseline, breaking this important service game and taking a 5-4 lead. He then won the next game.

Crawford deserved the victory. He was able to remain calm and steady during critical moments, not missing any shots, and placed his shots accurately. He was affected in the fourth set by being trapped in a bad situation in the third set and gradually became impatient, missing very easy shots. Sato made similar errors, double-faulting, sending shots into the net, and missing two easy smashes. He took risks by approaching the net and increasing his speed in the fourth set, which was surprising. This match was full of powerful shots. Crawford's performance was slightly inferior to Sato's at the end.

Andrew and Stenteman, who defeated Tonber and Questro, lost to Krahmn and Nona in four sets. They won the first set and tried hard to win the second and third sets but failed. Both Krahmn and Nona had powerful shots and good smashes, but Stenteman's serve was slightly weaker. Nona, who is black and small, is much worse than Krahmn, but his angle shots are particularly useful. Krahmn is good, but makes too many errors. Ms. Land and Sanshou Kanki defeated Ms. Kai and Tonber. Kai was much less impressive. Mrs. Gofre and Mrs. Mikel continued to win, defeating Mrs. Burke and Ms. Thomas in two sets.

Page 17

Chunqiu (Spring and Autumn)

What Happened to Yang Hengchun?

— Cheng Xiaoqing

Who is Yang Hengchun? He is an unknown person. His name only briefly appeared in the newspapers, so it's natural that he wouldn't leave much of an impression on people's minds. Now, I'll extract a short news item from the newspapers of August 6th as an introduction:

"Yesterday morning, a daytime robbery occurred in the City God Temple in the city... The victim, Wu Ma Shi, cried out for help, and the robbers shot and injured her left leg... At that moment, Yang Hengchun, a Shandong native and employee of the Xinyi Zhai bird shop on Liangting Road, heard the cries and gave chase, grabbing one of the robbers. He was also shot by another robber, the bullet hitting Yang Hengchun in a vital area. His life is in danger, and he has been sent to Tongren Hospital..."

What happened to Yang Hengchun? Did he die? Or was his gunshot wound fortunately healed? Is he still in the hospital? What is his current situation? I think about it every day, but there has been no follow-up in the newspapers! His name has never been revealed in the newspapers again!

In my humble opinion, Yang Hengchun's act of upholding justice and eliminating evil is of great significance. Mr. Yang and the robbed Wu Ma Shi were originally strangers. In the eyes of ordinary people, Wu Ma Shi's robbery was unrelated to Mr. Yang. However, from the perspective of social consciousness, the security of society is the responsibility of every citizen. In other words, every citizen should be responsible for suppressing evil and violence to maintain social order, just as every citizen has the sacred duty to defend the country in the face of national survival. Most unfortunately, when the crime occurred, other citizens were concerned about their own personal interests and abandoned their due obligations, standing idly by. Only Mr. Yang, relying on the legacy of chivalry from Qi and Lu, demonstrated the spirit of courage and righteousness on which national survival depends! Therefore, I believe that in this moment when national spirit is dim and depressed, Mr. Yang's actions are of great significance in terms of society, nation, and country and deserve praise and promotion.

We remember that local officials would personally attend the funeral of a police officer who died in the line of duty, and local public organizations would also commemorate and compensate a firefighter who sacrificed himself in the line of duty. But Mr. Yang's courageous actions are of even greater value and significance than those of public officials who die in the line of duty. His life and death deserve attention. But why are the wise local officials and enthusiastic social organizations so indifferent and silent? And why are those great columnists and reporters who pay attention to social news unwilling to spare a few words for this respectable and lovable hero, slightly investigating and describing him, after writing enthusiastically about "玉體橫陳" (jade body lying down) and "一絲不掛" (without a single thread), so-called social news? I dare say that this is the real social news! If this happened in Europe and America or neighboring islands, I believe that large headlines would occupy important space in the newspapers.

Finally, with twelve thousand percent sincerity, I offer the question in the title of this article to the wise officials, the reporters who guide public opinion, the leaders of society, local public organizations, and the general public of men and women with sound reason:

What happened to Yang Hengchun?

Right and Wrong

— Hu Liwen

When two people are arguing over the same thing, there is always "right" and "wrong." Either party A is "right" or party B is "right." Either party A is "wrong" or party B is "wrong." There is definitely no such thing as all "right" or all "wrong." However, the people who are arguing will never admit their own "wrong." They always say that they have their own reasons, showering the mediators with so many reasons that they become dizzy and don't know who is "right" and who is "wrong." Although they have good intentions to mediate, they don't have the vision to distinguish "right" and "wrong." As a result, they can only stand by and watch, letting them each insist on their own "right" and each deny their own "wrong."

After France occupied the Nine Islands, our country protested, and Japan also protested. Who is "right" and who is "wrong"? Originally, it could be distinguished by simply looking at the national history. But unfortunately, the Chinese are too indifferent. They don't even understand what their own things look like. Even if China's protest is not entirely "right" and Japan's protest seems "right" but is actually "wrong," the great figures who claim to uphold justice can only pretend to be ignorant and ignore "right" and "wrong." As a result, France recognizes Japan as "right" and appeases them, while recognizing China as "wrong" and turns its back on them.

Alas! In today's world, the strong are "right" and the weak are "wrong." How true these words are! How meaningful these words are!

On Lian

— Ti Gong

Wan Hua's disciple, Wei Lianfang, has just begun to show her talent. Zhou Lang of Shanghai seems quite melancholy about it. When I first saw her at a banquet at the Hong Kong Grand Theater, she was tall and slender, and I couldn't help but be intrigued. However, after watching her first performance of "Red Thread Stealing the Box," I couldn't help but sigh at my superficial judgment. Her voice is sweet and bright and sufficient, and her performance of mimicking Mei is already full of charm. Her two sword dances are as smooth as swimming dragons and as light as startled geese. Her waist and leg skills seem to require ten years of dedicated training. Judging by this, she can be considered the top of her class among those who study Mei today. And I believe that she is the one who will inherit Mei's legacy in the future.

Alleyway Chit-Chat

— Zui Chi Sheng (Drunken Fool)

After having dinner, I stood idly outside and felt the heat gradually dissipating. A gentle breeze blew against my clothes, naturally giving me a sense of comfort. At this time, the neighbors on the left and right, men and women, were all lined up cooling off in the alleyway. In this open-air gathering, one often hears descriptive and interesting conversations.

Sister-in-law Zhang said: I haven't seen Lingdi from next door for a long time. I guess she's gone back to her mother-in-law's house.

Sister-in-law Li said: Don't you know? She officially got married last month. I heard she became a second wife. The husband is in his thirties, has a good character, and is doing well financially. The funniest thing is that her grandmother sent a letter from Songjiang a few days ago, asking her to go back. She said there were few people at home and all the chores were waiting for the daughter-in-law to come back and take care of them. Little did she know that she had already become someone else's daughter-in-law. That old lady is still in the dark! Sister-in-law Zhang looked surprised and said: That's a joke. Someone like Lingdi would also change her mind and get married. She doesn't seem flamboyant or weird at all, but she's become free. It's like saying, "A cat that catches mice doesn't meow."

Sister-in-law Li said: You can't blame her. She's a young woman, just like a flower. When she was a bride, she was only eighteen years old. At that time, her husband already had tuberculosis, so she married him to ward off bad luck. Who knew that her husband would die after only two months? She's been a widow ever since, for six or seven years. I heard she's still a "Miss." In today's situation, Song Jie's morality doesn't make much sense. She's able to keep her eyes open and pick a man to marry and start over. That's her good fortune.

Sister-in-law Zhang's face seemed to turn a little red after hearing these words. She couldn't speak for a long time. It turns out she's also a widow "resolving to remain faithful until death"!

××××

At this time, Mr. Wang was listening and smiling. Sister-in-law Li turned the conversation and asked: Is your wife's illness any better today? I'm worried about her.

Mr. Wang said: Thank you. My wife saw a doctor yesterday, and after taking the medicine, her stomach feels a little lighter. And she's farted three times. The first time was at 9:40 last night. The second time was at one o'clock in the middle of the night. The third time was at dawn. Farting is a sign of qi flowing smoothly. So when I heard the fart, I felt relieved. Anyway, her illness is all caused by stagnation of liver qi. All said and done, it's our old lady's fault for having such a bad temper. She always likes to talk too much, regardless of whether her daughter-in-law is getting angry or not. So it's hard to avoid being troubled. There's also one annoying thing about our old lady. Every time she goes to sleep, she always coughs and spits phlegm. The sound of her wheezing and sighing never stops. She sleeps in the room next door, and it tires people out so much that they can't sleep soundly. How can someone who is sick sleep well? That's just fate.

Mr. Wang said goodbye again and went inside. Sister-in-law Li sighed: Alas... The old lady pants, not as good as the young mistress farting. "Old pearls are worthless," what else is there to say.

The Fourth Company Commander of the Northeast

— Zhang Henshui

Chapter 14: Difficulty in Finding a Wife, Hesitation and Worry About the Future, Small Gathering of Friends, Shy Remembrance of the Past

Zhao Ziqiang laughed: Where did you get those few sentences? You made them all up. Yin Deren didn't argue with him, but patted his shoulder and laughed: Hurry up and prepare for the wedding. It'll be spring soon. Besides the condolence money (Note: When something happy or sad happens to someone in the same battalion, officers from the brigade commander down give money as congratulations or condolences, called collective charity. The amount ranges from a few cents to a few yuan), I have to give you a generous gift, haha! Zhao Ziqiang saw that he wouldn't say anything, so he had to walk downstairs. But on the opposite wall, he saw the slogan that their company had prepared for the inspection committee: "If the Xiongnu are not wiped out, how can we have a home?" Zhao Ziqiang thought, just looking at this, Yin Deren's aspirations are clear. Looking at the affairs of Guan and Yin, it really doesn't make sense for soldiers to get married. In this day and age, if the guns aren't pointed outwards, they'll be pointed inwards. How long can they be stationed in this place in Xiyuan? It's impossible for a company commander to take his family everywhere. He can only leave his wife at home. If a young wife is left at home, can she avoid any problems in this day and age? Zhao Ziqiang asked himself the difficult questions and thought about them himself, and his heart grew cold. He just stared blankly at the eight-character slogan on the wall. Someone called out Zhao Company Commander beside him. When he turned around, it was the company's quartermaster standing there. He asked: Your company is even more well-organized, and the slogans are written so neatly. Who wrote them? The quartermaster said: I wrote them. Actually, our Company Commander Yin himself thinks these eight characters are right. Zhao Ziqiang also understood what he meant and shrugged his shoulders with a slight smile. The quartermaster said: Zhao Company Commander, when will I get to drink a cup of your wedding wine? Zhao Ziqiang laughed: You even know about this matter. Fortunately, this isn't a bad thing. If it were a bad thing, I couldn't keep it a secret. He laughed and walked back to the company headquarters, thinking to himself, can this marriage be done or not? I really should consider it now. Short Story

The Salesgirl

— Ke Ding'an

Zhu Xinong often saw many articles praising salesgirls in the tabloids, and she couldn't help but be extremely envious. One said how beautiful the Parker (nickname for salesgirls) of Chang Le Company was, another said how charming the stocking queen of Rong Guang Company was. Yet another said how delicate the bun beauty of Hua Qiang Company was, and how enchanting the silk head beauty of Ai Li Company was... All this made her feel very envious and at the same time very frustrated, because she had also looked at her own face in the clear mirror, carefully observed it, and found that it was well-grown and very full. Although it couldn't be said to be a round face replacing the moon, it could be said to be an apricot face full of spring. Just those two tender cheeks, she felt, had the chance to be broken with a puff of air; and those two captivating dimples were even more precious and worth a fortune. That small mouth that wasn't pouting or flat, just grew there, plus some dazzling lipstick, and any heterosexual friend who saw it would come and bow down to her pomegranate skirt... If my luck doesn't come, then I won't have such a good opportunity. If there was such an advertisement from major companies to recruit salesgirls, I would definitely win in the end... Such fragmented thoughts often lingered in her mind.

Our company now needs ten salesgirls to be assigned to various departments to serve. The remuneration is generous. If you are willing to come and serve, from × month × day to × month × day, from 1:00 PM to 3:00 PM, please come to the salesgirl registration office of Lili Company at 323 Huashi Road to contact us. Lili Co., Ltd.

This advertisement was published in the local news classified advertising column of Le Bao on × day. The wooden block characters: "Salesgirls Wanted" were arranged in front. What amazing news this was! Especially for our Zhu Xinong, she saw such a good message that fit her heart on that day, and of course she felt extremely happy.

This is an obvious fact: posting newspaper ads to recruit personnel attracts even more people than using candy to attract ants. This time, Lili Company also stated that it was from 1:00 PM to 3:00 PM, but at 9:00 AM, a middle-aged woman with long raindrop eyebrows and a thin figure came to apply. In the end, she left because the time had not yet arrived.

After they had lunch, they arranged three long tables in the style of three characters each in the salesgirl registration office, and put paper, ink, brushes and inkstones on them, waiting for the salesgirls to come for the exam. At that time, it was only 1:38 PM! Two girls of almost the same height, dressed in black clothes and white shoes, came in together. The staff managing the registration quickly stood up to greet them, asked them to sit down separately, and each fill out a registration form. However, the continuous arrival of applicants meant that the staff was not enough to manage them. Among the many people, of course there were beautiful ones and ugly ones. Among them was a pair of twin flowers, who said they had worked at Chang Le Company. One was wearing a long printed silk dress and had worked at the Sino-Foreign Pharmacy, one was wearing a long striped spun dress and had worked at the × District Office, and one was dressed as a student and had taught at ×× Middle School. There were quite a few who had done things and had experience, but there were also many who had not done anything. The funniest thing was an old one and a young one. The old one was probably more than forty years old, and the young one was only fourteen years old. The old man who accompanied her, who looked like her father, said: She is sixteen years old. Zhu Xinong also came to apply at that time. There were already many people writing at the registration office. The staff asked her to wait a moment. This was really something that made people feel very interested. Her spring-like face, which was both angry and happy, could simply overwhelm the group of beauties who came to apply. Their staff were all secretly discussing that this person would probably be selected. After a woman in a light blue and black floral dress had finished filling out the form, they quickly came to greet her and ask her to fill it out. Sure enough, she held the fountain pen she had brought and wrote very fluently, without stopping at all, which simply stunned the staff. One person next to her was the opposite of her, holding the pen but unable to write a single word. A week later, a small newspaper had a big headline: Lili Company's Queen Zhu Xinong... It seemed that there was no need to read any further.

Shen Bao National Goods Weekly

Forum

National Goods Enterprise and Safety Equipment

— Yang An

The Industrial and Commercial Management Association invited Ms. E.M. Hinder, a factory management expert, to give a lecture the day before yesterday. Ms. Hinder pays close attention to factory safety issues. What she said are the problems most commonly encountered by domestic product factories, which are indeed matters of life and death for domestic product factories. Ms. Hinder raised the following issues:

First, after workers have started working, factories immediately close their entrance gates tightly, even sealing them with tape, prohibiting anyone from entering or exiting.

Second, many goods and miscellaneous items are piled up at factory entrances, causing many difficulties for people coming and going.

Third, buildings are too simple and crude, or in disrepair.

Fourth, dangerous goods that easily cause disasters are arbitrarily piled up.

Fifth, fire-fighting equipment is not fully equipped.

Most factories still fail to pay attention to improving these situations, resulting in repeated tragedies. The recent catastrophe at the Zhengtai Rubber Factory and others is particularly frightening to think about. Factory safety equipment is the most important and noteworthy issue during the year of national goods. Ms. Hinder is extremely enthusiastic about this matter. When she lectured the other day, most leaders of various domestic product factories attended, demonstrating a consensus on this issue. At the same time, various factories in Shanghai have also organized an Industrial Safety Association, specializing in the research and improvement of industrial safety equipment, and publishing an Industrial Safety Monthly, introducing European and American works on industrial safety issues. This is truly a good phenomenon during the year of national goods. Mr. Wu Yun-chu said: "China is an industrially backward country. Due to a shortage of capital, factories mostly invest all their funds in production equipment, without considering whether this equipment is safe, let alone special safety equipment." This is such a heartbreaking matter. Many factory leaders should not assume that because they have been running their factories for one or two decades without experiencing a disaster, injury, or death, that they can be satisfied. This is just luck, not proof that safety equipment has been given attention or is irrelevant. If they are perfunctory and continue as before, the sacrifices will be immeasurable in the event of an accident. Therefore, I hope that the authorities of each factory will pay close attention to this major issue with all their strength, and not be too stingy with expenses. Stinginess often leads to greater losses. They should not rely solely on ideals, as ideals are merely empty talk. We should not run factories unless we are prepared to do so. The first priority in running a factory is to work steadily and cautiously. By paying attention to this issue, there is hope for the national goods enterprise.

National Goods Talk

An Analysis of the Contradictory Purchasing Power of the Chinese People

— Sheng Bi

Today, I believe that everyone in the country knows that China is a country that has lost its sovereignty and suffered humiliation. However, the Chinese people, as if drunk, not only have failed to sober up and get rid of bad habits, but seem to be even more intoxicated. The entire Chinese nation is trapped in a deep pit of mistakes and contradictions.

Now, focusing solely on clothing, men and women seen on the market, especially young men and women, almost all have foreign goods on their bodies, some even wearing foreign goods from head to toe. Considering our national obligations and responsibilities, living in China today, with the countryside bankrupt and the market so desolate, and with civil wars erupting here and there, we are exporting our sweat and blood abroad! With the economy bankrupt to this point, is wearing foreign goods still considered glorious or respectable? Doesn't our country have strong and beautiful fabrics? To be more aristocratic, there are still silks and satins to wear, which have more glory than foreign goods that are merely superficial. To put it more clearly: "Wearing domestic goods is the only way to have true glory and true respect! Only then can you fulfill your national responsibilities and obligations!"

Regarding what I have said above, the Chinese people should use their clear minds to analyze it carefully and quickly abandon this vanity of leaking rights and interests abroad! I predict with certainty: "If we continue to be vain like this, in the near future, the entire Chinese nation will be vain to the point of extinction!" Domestic goods are equally exquisite, so why bother?

Speaking of household appliances, the situation is somewhat different from what was said above. This is in the small bourgeoisie's homes, in the living room, in the room, you can always see a little foreign utensils, of course, you are using your own money, however, you need to understand that this is not about paying attention to equipment, it is no different from using to hurt yourself! Even in terms of diet, the use of foreign goods is also considerable. If anyone could calculate the daily expenses, the amount would surely be shocking!

In short, we have our purely practical domestic goods. In terms of purchasing power, we should try our best to buy domestic goods so that Chinese money can be used and reused within our own country, and not be earned by the two-faced, blue-eyed foreigners and sent abroad! Let them laugh at us, holding up blue grape wine and singing songs of victory.

National Goods and Salesmen

— Tian Ran

The day before yesterday, I met a manager of a famous domestic product factory. He said: Promoting domestic goods is certainly a very important task at present, but the vanguard of promoting domestic goods is the salesmen of the issuing house. If the salesmen are effective, there will be more customers and goods will sell well. If the salesmen are ineffective, no matter how good your products are or how low the prices are, general customers will still look away and ignore you. He said that in the store, I stipulate that salesmen must have the following six minimum standard habits:

(1) Smiling (2) Nodding in greeting (3) Having an equal perspective (4) Speaking softly and slowly (5) Saying "Goodbye, goodbye" (6) Saying "Take care, take care" Finally, he said that after these six points, I added a sentence, "What about non-salesmen? What about the non-salesman scope?" These words are really well said. Don't think it's old news, the economy of doing business is all in there.

The National Goods Weekly Department of Shenbao

National Goods Discussion

Promotion of National Goods and Restoration of Rural Purchasing Power

— Yi Hong

The Northeast has been lost for two years now. The lost land has not been recovered, how can we call ourselves a nation? Ordinary patriotic compatriots, although witnessing the depth of the national crisis and feeling the tension of the moment, have the will to love the country but lack the means to defend it. Resistance against Japan is the only way for the nation to save itself, and the production industry is where the lifeblood of the country lies. Therefore, developing industry and enriching national strength are even more important tasks. The national goods industry is at a time of survival and extinction, economic panic, and the national capital is like floating in the wind and rain. The southeast corner still has a vigorous and positive image. It is what we must regard as comforting after disappointment.

(1) The Seriousness of Rural Bankruptcy 丨 Since imperialism ravaged its ideal market with its surplus production, rural handicrafts have been completely destroyed. The self-sufficient economic organization has been fundamentally shaken, and the national industry has been unable to develop due to heavy pressure. The old economic organization has been destroyed, and the new foundation has not yet been established. In this major transition between the old and the new, the various phenomena caused by rural bankruptcy are naturally inevitable stages in the process. Therefore, in addition to striving to establish a national industry and develop national capital, we have no other way to achieve self-reliance. However, there is one prerequisite, which is how to get rid of the shackles of imperialism and the oppression of feudal forces. (2) The Greatest Efforts of the National Goods Industry 丨 Promoting national goods is the main factor in developing national goods, and the greatest need is also the important target of promoting national goods. Farmers in our country account for 79% of the total population. What farmers need is the same as what the whole country needs. Since we recognize that the main consumers of national goods production are farmers, the direction of our efforts is naturally the countryside rather than the city. However, in recent years, rural areas have gone bankrupt, disasters have been frequent, and last autumn there was a "cheap grain hurt farmers" situation again. Ordinary farmers were already exhausted and unable to survive. The so-called purchasing power has plummeted to the lowest limit. It is not easy for us to promote national goods into the countryside and use them to prosper. Speculators only care about current interests and manufacture luxury goods one after another in order to cater to the tastes of urban society. This kind of deformed development is more harmful than beneficial to the future of the national industry. Although, we should not be sad about the harsh environment, and we should not be disappointed by the obstacles to progress. We must explore the root of the problem. Dare to ask if this road is absolutely impassable?

(3) How to Promote Rural Purchasing Power 丨 Rural purchasing power is so weak, but in fact, foreign goods are everywhere in the inland villages. It can be seen that the minimum necessities of farmers' lives are indispensable. Even if they are heavily in debt, they still try their best to handle it. How can they endure the destruction of capitalism after such exhaustion and exhaustion? Therefore, although purchasing power in inland villages is weak, the need cannot be reduced at any time. If the national goods industry can replace them, the prosperity of national goods can be expected and the outflow of profits can be avoided. What we should pay close attention to now is how to recover the rural market. Based on my humble opinions, I will list the following:

(A) Improvement of the quality of national goods and reduction of costs 丨 The goods required by farmers must have three conditions: cheap, good quality, and durable 丨 When the three are available, there will be great help in promoting the promotion.

(B) Investigation of foreign goods sales and manufacture of national goods substitutes 丨 Start with rural areas with convenient transportation, and investigate in detail their sales volume and distribution, and compile statistics for reference in the manufacture of national goods. The most popular ones should be imitated and manufactured as much as possible, and the government should be requested to exempt them from taxes, and strive to publicize them in order to drive foreign goods out of the market. After the advent of national goods such as tobacco, MSG, soap, and enamel products, the enemy goods disappeared invisibly, which is also the most remarkable achievement in the past.

(C) Establishment of the National Goods Production Chain Association 丨 Farmers have shallow knowledge and do not know how to choose when shopping, and are easily deceived by hypocrites. We should guide the organization of consumer cooperatives and jointly organize production and marketing associations with national goods factories and companies in urban areas, so that when farmers purchase, the goods are genuine and the prices are fair, and they know what to do, and avoid the exploitation of merchants.

(D) Deepening National Goods Exhibitions 丨 Poor rural areas are limited by their knowledge. National goods factories should contact and organize mobile exhibition groups, and conduct mobile exhibitions in rural villages to introduce them to farmers as much as possible, so that they have a considerable understanding of national goods and improve their faith.

The above four points are just the big ones. Finally, we should understand that this kind of policy to improve purchasing power is passive rather than active, and it is a symptomatic treatment rather than a cure. The real improvement of purchasing power can only be sound and lasting after the entire agricultural economic problem is solved. In addition to making considerable efforts for this kind of passive policy at present, we must also make long-term struggles to fundamentally get rid of the shackles of imperialism and build a stable national industry.
