Free Talk

Rare Books of the Complete Library of the Four Treasuries

— Rong Zhi Yu

Now, in addition to wars and political disputes, there is also a dispute over the phototype printing of "rare books" in the "Complete Library of the Four Treasuries" that few idlers would pay attention to. Officials and merchants want to print it in the original style as soon as possible, but the academic community believes that the library version has deletions and errors. If other versions are available, other "good versions" should be used instead.

However, the academic community's proposal will not pass, and the result will always be to follow the "Imperial Edition of the Complete Library of the Four Treasuries." The reason is very clear, just because they want to hurry. The disappearance of the four provinces and the sale of the nine birds are nothing to talk about. Just the Huanghe River's out-of-control actions make people feel that it is difficult to end the day. If you want to do business, you have to hurry. Moreover, the words "Imperial Edition" still have a bit of prestige. "Imperial Physician" and "Tribute Satin" have different meanings from others. Even France, which has long been a republic, Napoleon's collection of books is still more valuable than the collections of commoners at auction. The famous European "China scholars" will cite the "Imperial Edition of the Complete Library Integration" when talking about China. This is something that Chinese textual researchers are unwilling to play with, but it can also be seen that the "rare books" that have been printed with the "Imperial Edition" can always be better business than "good versions" abroad.

Even in China, I am afraid that the "rare books" are still better business. Because this can be used as decoration. And the "good version" can only be practical. Those who can buy such books are definitely not poor scholars who can afford it, so it is also conceivable that they will definitely be offered in the living room after they buy them. This kind of buyer will buy an ancient tripod from the Shang and Zhou dynasties and put it up. If necessary, they may buy a fake ancient tripod and put it up, but they will never buy a casserole or iron pot and put it on a rosewood table. Because his purpose is in "rare" and not in "good", and even less in whether it can be practical.

People in the late Ming Dynasty liked fame, and engraving ancient books was also a trend. However, they often did not understand it themselves. They thought it was a typo, so they changed it randomly. It would be okay not to change it, but once it was changed, it would be changed wrong, so that later textual researchers sighed and said that the Ming people liked to engrave ancient books, but the ancient books were lost. This time, the "rare books" in the "Complete Library of the Four Treasuries" are phototype printed, and there is absolutely no malpractice of changing mistakes. However, the original version has unintentional typos and deliberate deletions and changes, and because of the spread of the new version, it can make the good version sink down. If serious readers occasionally get such a copy in the future, I am afraid they will always have to sigh for the second time.

However, the result will always be to follow the "Imperial Edition of the Complete Library of the Four Treasuries." Because the affairs of "the future" are not related to the current officials and merchants.

Suzhou People and Lullabies

— You Sheng

At dusk, on Guanqian Street in Suzhou, you can often see a crowd of heads under the electric lights, staring blankly at the door plaques of the big merchants. A soft voice is released on the door plaque, like rice soup: "Uuuuuu········· 丨丨" This is the radio broadcasting Chen Yumei's lullaby. The crowd of heads is glued together by the sound waves, neither shaking nor making a sound. Their eyes are open, but they all seem to be asleep.

Chen Yumei's lullaby was transmitted to Suzhou, originally relying on "a polished black circle, with a dog drawn in front of a loudspeaker."

This time, every household is learning to sing it. The Wu people, who are good at soft words, have a special talent for the integration of this song's tune. Although the young masters also hum, they still find it comfortable to listen to and bite on melon seeds.

In this silent China, the lullaby can be regarded as the voice of Suzhou people. Because the two have absolute harmony in any aspect.

In life, let's look at the collection place that represents the important life of Suzhou people丨丨teahouse, the scene inside is the most serious. Tea guests surround the square table from morning to night, from morning to night. Neurologically speaking, Suzhou people do not go home all year round, hiding in the teahouse, Dragon Well tea, Sparrow Tongue tea, savoring it endlessly. It seems that their souls are wandering in the bottom of the cup and their bodies are in the pot. Although there is a noisy sound rolling, it is equal to snoring and talking in sleep. There is no lullaby singing here, but it contains a strong lullaby atmosphere. This air floats freely, filling the entire city of Suzhou.

In this "cradle" of Suzhou, there are sleeping Cheng Jian Aliutou; there is also our General Su Bingwen sleeping. (The general is now lying in ambush in Su)

Suzhou is originally the most suitable and should be a place to sleep. Even without listening to lullabies.

When my fellow villagers say that someone is sleeping, they do not say the word "sleeping": "Going to Suzhou"丨Because Suzhou is the place where straw mats are produced. Since there is a historical tradition, it is no wonder that the rich and important people now say that Suzhou is a very quiet place; isn't it best to sleep in quiet? What's wrong with changing the city of Suzhou to "Sleepy City"?

Moreover, the lullabies sung by the women of Suzhou are very pleasant!

Mr. Lin Yutang expressed his opinion a few days ago: "Let the women do it for a while!" He himself plans to step down and go abroad, and not hear about foreign affairs. (The Analects are still to be compiled, right?) This proposal is very purposeful for all men. Although Mr. Yu Ming explained that "women are also not good" and quoted the saying "Those who care for their health are not enough to handle major events" to criticize Mr. Yutang for only knowing how to read the Analects but not knowing how to read Mencius. However, Mr. Yu Ming did not think deeply about it······ If all the women sing in unison: "Don't quarrel, don't make noise, baby, take a nap, oh丨丨丨" Naturally, they will fall asleep, and even the women themselves will have a good sleep, and a major event in life will be completed. Then listen: "Asleep, awake, get up and eat a piece of cake······" Cake, no matter what kind of cake, is always better than tree bark and grass roots, right? 200 million people just "urge," and 200 million people just "sleep." As a result, everyone is sleeping. If you want the world to be uneasy, how can you get it? Therefore, I say: To govern the world with sleep, success can be achieved immediately.

By the way, if there are women in the country who do not understand how to sing lullabies, they can ask the people of Suzhou; men who are hypnotized but do not sleep can also ask the people of Suzhou. Suzhou people, in China, that is, in the world, they are all thoroughly proficient in hypnosis and sleep, and they are also very polite to hope for them.

The Story of the Wind

— Sun Yang

Because the house I live in is already old and cannot stand firmly, I felt uneasy when I read in the newspaper a few days ago that there would be strong winds coming to Shanghai. I worried all night, but fortunately the wind did not come.

But my "wind" is open, and in the past, Song Yu and Jing Cha accompanied King Xiang of Chu to visit the Lantai Palace. A wind blew suddenly, and King Xiang was very happy and said: "How pleasant! Is this wind shared by me and the common people?" Song Yu hurriedly replied: "This is only the wind of the great king!" Then he showed his "helping idleness" talent and described the wind of the great king: At first, this wind started from the foot of Mount Tai: "Fluttering and surging, exciting and angry; overturning stones and cutting down trees, killing the forest and running." First, it started out with great power outside the imperial city, and then "riding over the high city and entering the deep palace." After circling a few times, only the tail of the wind was left, blowing on King Xiang's belly, of course, it was happy.

Song Yu's flattery was very appropriate. Jing Cha could only be dry and embarrassed. Qu Yuan hid at the bottom of the Miluo River, probably regretting that he was too honest and not as good as a disciple. Thousands of years later, Li Houzhu was ignorant and "busy himself," and suffered disaster with "the small building was blown by the east wind again last night." Compared with Song Yu, Yu really deserves to be the master of describing the wind! Since there is the wind of the great king, there must be the wind of the common people. Song Yu said that this wind originated in the poor alley, "moving sand and dust, blowing dead ashes, alarming the dirty water, and raising rotten waste." Blowing into the nostrils, it must be uncomfortable. Compared with the wind of the great king "wandering among cinnamon and pepper," it is no wonder that King Xiang was complacent. However, Song Yu did not pay attention to the fact that when the wind of the great king was showing its power outside the city, the common people had already suffered enough. Thanks to King Xiang being confused丨丨or even pretending to be confused丨丨otherwise Song Yu would be in trouble.

Pretending to be confused is appropriate, and flattery is popular, but I feel that the wind of the great king has a bit of the "push" flavor of the "third kind of people." This is just like the wind that had not yet blown to the Bund buildings a few days ago, stirring up a big fire in the grassy mud pond of Laobaidu in Pudong, burning down the thatched sheds of two thousand poor people.

I also thought that if the big storm that bypassed Shanghai really came, what kind of wind could it be? In vulgar terms, it is a tornado, and in elegant terms, according to the writing style of "helping idleness" literati, it can only be regarded as the wind of the committee chairman. Fortunately, this wind only circled in the southern part of the East China Sea and went straight to Korea without going to Japan.

So I was doubly relieved!

Autumnal Thoughts

— Zhou Lengjia

It is autumn once more.

The wind blows in from outside the window, adding to the coolness I feel.

I can't help but recall past events:

It was also such an autumn when I accompanied my weeping wife, carrying the coffin of our eight-month-old child, together to the International Cemetery.

The child had died of acute cholera.

Watching helplessly as three or four coolies buried the child's coffin, every subtle sound struck deeply into my heart. My heart ached intensely. Tears fell to the ground like coins, mingling with my wife's tears.

The child's voice and smiling face had vanished forever. I thought of the past eight months, as if I had lived a beautiful dream. Now, the dream was over, and all that remained for me was pain and sorrow, nothing else.

Silently, I placed a wreath on the child's grave, with these words attached to it: "May your innocent soul rest peacefully in heaven!"

On the way back, my heart was cold, as cold as the autumn wind.

Today, I feel this same cold wind again, and it suddenly reminds me: it is the child's first death anniversary.

I put down the work in my hands and ran out to buy a wreath, taking a car to the International Cemetery.

Standing before the child's grave, I felt lost. I thought about the events of the past year.

This is truly a time of drastic change. I have never seen the wheels of time turn so quickly. Under these wheels, the countryside is collapsing rapidly, our rivers and mountains continue to be shattered, the Yellow River is overflowing its banks, the people, on the verge of death, are crying out, and the fallen class is dancing madly on skulls. As for me, squeezed into the middle class, I am fortunate enough to still be alive. This is truly lucky.

But the child is also fortunate: he did not die in a dark corner, buried in a dark corner, unseen, unremembered, and he can receive the wreath I offer him.

Silently, I placed a wreath on the child's grave, sincerely praying:

"May your innocent soul rest peacefully in heaven!"

Woman (7)

— Shen Congwen

She didn't need to understand these things. After moving into a famous seaside hotel, she spent her days quietly lying under a white parasol on the beach, gazing at the bright blue of the sea and sky. She was using the scenery of Beihai to wash away the unpleasant impressions of the South China Sea that lingered in her mind. She was resting. She was waiting.

Sometimes she hired a white horse and rode around the mountains, or along the sandy beaches, deserted by bathers, where the tide had receded. At other times, she would sit alone in a small boat, slowly rowing with small oars, taking the boat three or five li out to sea, letting it drift and sway on the salty water.

The unfamiliar place and unfamiliar people did not make her feel lonely. In this quiet and undisturbed solitude, she had a companion: her own heart.

When she lay on the sand, she seemed to understand nature and her own nature a little better. She seemed to see everything, hear everything, and analyze everything with greater clarity than before.

What particularly pleased her was that, in this place, among the tourists, no one seemed to know who she was. Although there seemed to be several pairs of unfamiliar eyes that might accidentally meet hers on the beach each day, and she even suspected that these eyes often watched her from afar and from hidden places, there was no trouble. Even if a woman is tired of men, she often, in her consciousness, remembers the impression of men acting foolishly because of her beauty. As a kind of secret pleasure… of course we cannot like a person who loves wine, but a drunkard in a writer's work does not make us frown. In this world, there are also several kinds of human postures of those who are captivated by beauty, which are smiling when they are presented!

Rowing was a sport that she was good at, and the surface of ×× Sea was especially suitable for light boats to float on in the morning and evening. One day, she drove that white boat alone, paddling with oars, and sailed east along the coast.

The east is the place where the sun rises, and there should also be things as bright and passionate as the sun waiting there. But what was she waiting for?

In the east, apart from two pyramid-shaped islands ten miles away, there was only a sea plated with silver by the sunlight. The sea was silver in the morning and blue in the afternoon, emitting the brilliance of blue sapphires. The vast sea filled one with boundless fantasies.

A little further east, there were two more bays, also with sandy beaches, suitable for sea bathing, but with very few visitors.

She slowly rowed the boat, thinking until she reached the third bay. She liked to look at the scenery on the coast from the boat. She liked playing so lonely, because she was tired of being lively.

Securities

August Futures Bond Delivery Proceeds Very Smoothly

A total of 31,235,000 yuan

Yesterday (August 30th) was the delivery date for August futures at the Chinese Securities Exchange. Because it was summer, the number of trading sessions was reduced, and the market was closed every afternoon. From the 21st, it was changed to three sessions. In addition, the situation in this month was calm, without any major changes, so the trading was also greatly reduced. However, the amount of delivery was not less than before, and the process was quite smooth. It was found that the total amount of delivery was 31,235,000 yuan, of which 15,955,000 yuan was settled and delivered by the brokers themselves through mutual account transfers. The amount of delivery in the exchange was 15,280,000 yuan. However, although the amount of off-exchange delivery by the brokers was impossible to verify, it should also be several million yuan. The largest amount of delivery was still from No. 46 in the financial sector, with approximately 6-7 million delivered. A certain bank received approximately 5-6 million in goods, and the remaining entry and exit quantities were approximately 1 million or so, with the smallest amount being only over 100,000. The northern gang also delivered, and the number of arbitrage was also considerable. The market price was very stable, with fluctuations mostly within one yuan, and the smallest being only 5 fen or 1 jiao. The flatter the market price, the less the transaction. It was found that on August 18th, the entire day's trading was only 2,920,000, which shows how quiet the market was. Tracing back to June 30th, the initial market price of the August futures was 63 yuan and 4 jiao for disarmament. The smallest price in the middle was 62 yuan and 9 jiao on July 4th, and the highest was 68 yuan on July 19th. Although the difference between the highest and lowest was 5 yuan and 1 jiao, when calculated in August, the highest was 67 yuan and 5 jiao, and the lowest was 65 yuan and 1 jiao, with a difference of only 2 yuan and 1 jiao. The difference between the highest and lowest salt tax was 5 yuan and 2 jiao, which was only 2 yuan and 5 jiao when calculated in this month. There were 58 days in between, and the most memorable was only July 19th, because the US-China loan was established on July 5th, and the market was filled with shorts, and the rising trend was extremely large, until July 19th. After August, the bond market was dull and lifeless. On August 1st, Chief Chiang's telegram to Chahe was peaceful, and on August 7th, Feng's telegram withdrew from Cha Province. The situation came to an end. Although rumors were spread that Doolan had fallen again, Japan had demanded old debts, or that the government would issue new bonds, they were all nothing but baseless rumors. Therefore, the market price in this month was generally in a state of steady consolidation. Moreover, before and after delivery, it was as usual, with no signs of squeezing shorts or longs. Therefore, August had almost no special circumstances to speak of. Only 961 kind suddenly rumored reorganization on August 23, and saw some fluctuations, but it was only a flash in the pan. The future may wait for Finance Minister Song to announce his new contributions after returning home before there will be a larger wave. Cotton 3,300 packages, yarn 37,500 dans

The Bombay cotton market firmed up due to purchases by a small number of retail investors and speculators. As a result, Pinga'er rose by 1 rupee 2.5 jiao, Tianmula rose by 1 rupee 1.5 jiao, and Bailuoxi rose by 1 rupee 1.75 jiao. The original telegram is recorded to the left. (Dated 29th)

Grains

Flour Speculation Rampant

丨This month, horizontal jump of two-thirds of a cent丨

Yesterday morning, after the opening of the flour market, the prices of each month showed a sign of initial softness followed by a rise. Due to the price of foreign wheat continuing to fall by $1.12 in Chicago and about 34 cents in Canada, the sentiment was not good at the initial opening. However, because this month was the last day, the general short positions were frantically covering, and the factories were also recovering their chips. Therefore, amidst the cheap spot prices, a squeeze was formed. Hence, this month rose steadily. Distant months were also slightly pulled up. By the afternoon opening, the squeeze on this month was still severe. It was rumored that some end-user accounts declared to the factories that they would buy, and the goods had been shipped out, but the standard had not yet been covered, so they had to rush in at the end. Therefore, the highest squeeze at the fourth session reached $2.28, but because the market price for August and September had leveled, hedging returned, and factories dumped about 200,000 bags, the situation became peaceful. It was found that this month's squeeze was not due to a shortage of goods, but entirely caused by short positions. As a result, this month rose horizontally by two-thirds of a cent compared to the previous day, September rose by 1.7 cents, October and November rose by 2.5 cents, December remained unchanged, and January rose by 2.5 cents.

Wheat Follows and Rises Five to Six Cents

Yesterday, after the noon opening of the wheat futures market, the prices of each month showed a sign of initial flatness followed by a rise. Due to the decline in foreign wheat quotations, the opening price in September saw a small correction. Afterwards, each session rose because the flour market turned higher and because of Mr. Cai Song's return to China and the fact that the wheat had not yet been purchased, which caused concern. Therefore, each month showed a positive trend. By the afternoon opening, the market sentiment for each month had become peaceful, with little change compared to the morning. However, there are still abundant inventories of flour and wheat, so there are still problems in the future. As a result, September rose by six cents compared to the previous day, October rose by five cents, November rose by five cents, December rose by six cents, and January rose by four cents. Spot wheat is still active, but the quality of the goods varies, and the prices also fluctuate greatly. Qintong wheat opened at $3.79, Wuhe wheat at $3.89, and Yaowan wheat at $3.85, down to $3.75. Yangzhou wheat opened at $3.57, down to $3.20. Zhenjiang wheat opened at $3.38, and Gaoyou wheat opened at $3.67, down to $3.55, totaling 7,000 bags, it is said.

New Kexian Rice from Fujian Sells Very Actively

Changan Autumn Silkworms Cocooning

Hardware

Hardware Market Lifeless

Recently, the hardware market has been showing a sluggish and difficult-to-revive trend. The trade in the northern route has been affected by the Yellow River breach and has become exhausted. The Yangtze River route, such as Anqing, Nanjing, Hankou, and Wuhu, still has some demand, but the number is limited. The formerly popular Jiujiang and Nanchang ports have been affected by the military situation (suppression of communists) and the trade is unremarkable. There is also little trade in Fujian and Zhejiang. Local factories in this port have also been very few recently, leading to an almost standstill in the entire market. It can be said to be the most deserted era in recent years. As a result, the standards of various goods have mostly declined. For example, tinplate, bamboo steel, blue lead, pure antimony, steel, and other varieties are all in a downward trend. There is not a single variety that is improving. Although there is an upward trend in spot tin, it is out of stock and there is no market. Other than that, there is nothing to report.

Taihu: produced in Taihu, Anhui. The goods are mixed in quality. The size and shape are the same as Macheng. The outer packing is also the same. The annual production is about 8,000 to 9,000 dan.

Commentary

"Stealing" and "Robbing"

— Yin

丨Reply to Mr. "Ganxu" on "Talking About Poverty"丨

Not long ago, I talked about "poverty" in this publication. What I meant was: "Poverty" is the most stimulating and fulfilling life; only by going through the class of "poverty" can there be permanent, great, and true creation. However, many "poor people" cannot bear the hardship of "poverty" and go "stealing" and "robbing," which is their great mistake in viewpoint and action. Because after "stealing" and "robbing," they are no longer "poor," and they can rely on it to be fed, clothed, and enjoy themselves. However, in fact, the personal warmth, food, and enjoyment gained from their "stealing" and "robbing" will not benefit more people other than the few who carried out the "stealing" and "robbing." Instead, it will add a few more vigorous bosses to the "poverty" manufacturing plant. So, fundamentally, this is a reactionary, erroneous, narrow, incomplete, and individualistic concept! There are also those who cannot conquer the "suffering" of "poverty" and commit suicide. This is truly the most contemptible, shameful, and weak ugliness exposed! Because they do not understand that "poverty" is a raging flame that can burn out passionate, upward, and dynamic emotions. They do not understand that "poverty" is the lighthouse of a fulfilling life, illuminating us to strive and create practically on the journey of life. Of course, they will not know the cause of the "poverty" illness and where to diagnose the "poverty" pulse. I believe that my words are not entirely empty words divorced from reality, because the world revolutionary writer Gorky was completely beaten in the waves of "poverty" thousands or even countless times and finally succeeded.

The day before yesterday, in this publication, Mr. "Ganxu," because a friend also committed suicide in the Hong Kong current in front of the "Cannot Die" sign on Yanziji, used it as evidence to counter my argument. The reason is: His friend is indeed weak, but if his friend could "steal" and "rob," he would not have committed suicide by throwing himself into the river. Finally, he also proposed that "stealing" and "robbing" are the "instincts" of "human beings," not "shameful" and "promising" slogans.

In fact, this evidence will never become evidence. The reason is, I have already explained it in "Talking About Poverty." The previous paragraph of this article also said a bit. Now, let me add some more. Let's take Mr. "Gan" 's friend as an example: Assuming that Mr. "Gan" 's friend really went "stealing" and "robbing" as Mr. "Gan" imagined, then, it is not a question that his friend will not die in vain, but he is also full of hope of getting rich, at least, hope of personal warmth, food, and enjoyment. From then on, he personally is a happy person who is no longer "poor" and no longer "suffering"! However, what are the benefits for the public? ... And assuming that this is indeed a method of chasing away "poverty" and eliminating "suffering," then the "poor people" will all go their own way to bury themselves in this "stealing" and "robbing" that can lead to personal warmth, food, and enjoyment. Then, of course, all the passionate, upward, and dynamic creative emotions will be shattered, the light on the "lighthouse" will be extinguished, the fire in the "furnace" will be extinguished, and the front line of striving and advancing will be eased and eventually shaken. The future, in addition to the pursuit of personal "stealing" and "robbing," is still personal "stealing" and "robbing"! The world becomes a reactionary, erroneous, incomplete, and individualistic world! ...

But, but Mr. "Gan" 's friend is still a contemptible, promising weakling in front of the "Cannot Die" sign on Yanziji!

Finally, from "stealing a country" to "stealing a hook," it is proven that this is a world of "stealing" and "robbing" robbers. However, I do not believe that "stealing" and "robbing" is the inevitable reflection of "poverty" in action. What's more, I deny that it is the "instinct" of "human beings"!

Everyone Has a Jealous Heart

— Zhen Zhi

Mencius said, "The heart of compassion is possessed by all." The meaning of this sentence seems to be that if people see something tragic, they will naturally feel compassion. However, I don't think so. A beggar follows behind a well-dressed, wealthy young man, calling him "young master" repeatedly, hoping that he will show some compassion and give him a copper coin. What happens? He follows him for a long way and is subjected to curses like "Get out of here," "Pig," and "Annoying." From this, it seems that asking for people's compassion is clearly not easy. Furthermore, our country, because it lost the three northeastern provinces, begged for the compassion of the League of Nations, but the result was the same as the beggar and the wealthy young man. This further proves that "seeking compassion from others" is impossible. So "the heart of compassion is possessed by all" becomes a generality. I want to change the generality into a reality, so I rashly changed it to "everyone has a jealous heart," which is also for a good reason.

Literature and Art

Lamenting the Yellow River

— Chang Zunxian

The Yellow River collapses, inundating Mount Hua and Song,

The Fen River flows west, the Ji River east,

The rushing, overturning sea is powerful and surging,

People and objects are like mountains, terrifying dragons,

The whole family sleeps in one house at night,

Swept by the waves into the whale's belly,

One hundred li away, the sound of flying waves can still be heard,

Near, one cannot hear the sound of people crying,

One only sees corpses floating with the waves,

Birds pecking at backs, fish hitting heads,

Wanting to salvage, the water is rapid, difficult to row,

Standing alone in the setting sun, tears streaming down,

Year after year, sighing at the suffering of the sand fields,

Blood and flesh in a mess, fattening jackals and tigers,

Du's bones are still rotting in the soil,

How can they rot with the drifting sand?

It is said that warlords are inherently unkind,

Why is the River God not merciful and called a god?

If it is said that the calamity is destined by Heaven,

Why do all the innocent people die?

Raising my head, I ask Yu Chen,

The potters and modelers lost their great balance,

Dumb springs, disastrous waters,

Why not sink together?

Is there no virtue to make up for it,

Why does Royal Heaven not care?

Why are you not respectful, and my heart does not submit?

There is much idle happiness in half a hall,

Don't you hear the carriages and horses come and go, the sound of police clearing the way,

Without sorrow, one song rests the mountains and crouches. (Instead of reward)

People only know that the two words "jealousy" are used exclusively for disputes between the sexes, fighting, etc., but they do not know what ingredients form the elements of "jealousy." Some say that of course oxygen is the main element, but what raw materials are used to make oxygen? They can't answer when asked directly. In fact, it's very easy. It's nothing more than the raw materials created under the "not wanting others to touch what you love." In other words, this is oxygen. From that oxygen, apart from the jealousy that should exist in the disputes and fights between the sexes, we can say that the pursuit of fame and profit by merchants and villagers cannot be separated from the ingredients of jealousy. The power struggles and money scraping of adults and gentlemen cannot be separated from the ingredients of jealousy, because based on the principle of raw materials forming, it can be believed without a doubt.

Vinegar is a must-eat, because it comes with life. Why is that? Don't you often see rape cases in the newspaper... disputes... fights (for women)... etc., all of which are enough to show that vinegar is innate. Then, merchants love money, buy Japanese goods, adults love money, scrape the people's fat, are inevitable. So I changed "the heart of compassion is possessed by all" to "everyone has a jealous heart," doesn't it seem more appropriate!

Current Celebrity Paintings and Calligraphy

(Brief Biography)

Qian Baohe, style name Zhongliang, also known as Er Nan Shang, is 64 years old, from Wuxi. He is a literary elder, skilled in poetry, lyrics, calligraphy, and painting, especially good at painting plum blossoms, with a vigorous and clear brush, free from current trends. His taste is between Xuehu and Yuji. In his early years, he served as an official in Guangdong and Jiangsu provinces, serving as a magistrate in arduous duties, with outstanding virtuous reputation. Recently, he established the Red Leaf Society in Shanghai, advocating elegance and discussing calligraphy and painting. Many of his society friends are well-known figures of the time.

A Proper Match

"Miss Peiying in the × mansion is getting more beautiful than before. Relying on her natural intelligence, she is only seventeen years old this year and has already graduated from high school. In the near future, she will go abroad to study at a university and will definitely bring back very glorious female doctorate, master, and bachelor's degrees, returning in great style. Let's see which young master will be lucky enough to marry this talented and beautiful daughter as his wife." The people in × town were all thinking like this in their minds. Mr. × and his wife have also spent many years of hard work on the marriage of Peiying, this "pearl in their palm." Although many people have come to propose marriage, they always consider it carefully, hoping to choose a family that is "a proper match," so that their beloved daughter's lifelong happiness will not be delayed.

Today, another wave of "Peiying's marriage problem" rose in Mr. ×'s heart. He thought that his daughter's age was not too young, and that she had already graduated from high school. On the principle of "a man should marry when he is old, and a woman should marry when she is old," Peiying's lifelong happiness could no longer be delayed. There have been many proposals of marriage these two days, so he must choose a good one to agree to, so that he can fulfill a kind of responsibility as a parent. Thinking of this, he hurried in to discuss it with his wife.

"Madam, I think Peiying's age is not too young. As the ancients said, 'A man should marry when he is old, and a woman should marry when she is old.' Recently, many families have come to propose marriage, so we should choose one that is 'a proper match' as soon as possible, so that we can fulfill our own worries."

His wife agreed with him and replied: "Old Master, you are right. Our children's marriages are indeed the heavenly duty of parents, and we should arrange her lifelong happiness as soon as possible, which also fulfills our responsibility. What's more, if we delay any longer, she is studying at school, and now there is a lot of talk about free love outside every day. I'm afraid Peiying will also see it and follow suit. Like the girl from the Wang family next door who eloped with someone last year and caused trouble, we would lose all face."

"Yes! But which of the families that have come to propose marriage recently do you think is good? We'll discuss it and reply to them." Mrs. × lowered her head and thought silently for a while. "As I see it, the Xu family's child is good. He is born extraordinarily handsome, and I heard that his knowledge is not bad, but his family is a bit poor, not good enough for our family! The one with the surname Lu is a better match. His family has more than 10,000 mu of land, and he has a lot of savings. Although the young master's talent is a bit worse, Peiying will not have a hard time marrying there. What do you think?"

Mr. × shook his head and said: "Wrong! I heard that the Lu family's child is not only ignorant and bad-tempered, but he has also become addicted to opium, so I don't agree with him very much!"

"Old Master, you are wrong. As long as a person has plenty of food and clothing in this world, what does it matter what knowledge and learning they have? What's more, people in the world today all 'value clothing over people'. If you have money, people will respect you. If you have knowledge, who will care about you! Speaking of his family's young master being addicted to opium, I think he has millions of dollars of wealth, so he doesn't have to worry about eating himself poor. And as the saying goes, 'A rich man eating opium protects his family property,' so smoking is irrelevant!"

Mr. × was enlightened by his virtuous wife's explanation of worldly affairs. In addition, he thought of the four words "a proper match," so he said happily: "Let's do it that way! Although he is an opium addict, he is still 'a proper match,' hehe."

Store Clerk Correspondence

How to Solicit Donations?

Editor Sir:

Many readers encounter difficult problems, and once they seek your guidance, you readily provide instructions, resolving many dire situations. This is a truly commendable thing. Since you possess the ability to compassionately guide and rescue people from hardship, I trust you will accept my request and be happy to advise me.

My hometown is in She County, southern Huizhou. I came to Shanghai at a young age and have been apprenticed in a cloth store. Time flies, and it has been more than a decade. However, the compensation I receive as an apprentice is never sufficient. Fortunately, I am thrifty and manage to support my family with the meager income I earn through hard work, enduring this difficult life. I deeply feel the weight of my efforts.

The situation is as follows: Last month, I received a letter from my hometown stating that on the 14th day of the fifth month, torrential rain suddenly fell in the southern She County area, causing flash floods. The floodwaters surged like galloping horses, and the water depth on flat ground reached over ten feet. In an instant, the area became a waterlogged land, submerging fields and collapsing houses. The cries of the displaced people and the floating corpses were a tragic sight. The disaster was unprecedented in its severity. My family lives there and has suffered the same misfortune, with the affected area filled with corpses. Upon receiving this news, those of us living abroad were extremely distressed. After the local authorities reported the details to the provincial government, a month passed, and there was still no relief plan. Therefore, the village elders discussed and initiated the "She County Fifth District Flood Relief Association." The initiators are responsible for fundraising, hoping to gather small contributions to save the lives of those who have survived. Just the day before yesterday, I received a donation booklet from the association, urging me to quickly raise funds from abroad to meet urgent needs.

Sir, rescuing those in distress is a natural duty, especially when it involves our hometown. Considering the bond of kinship, it becomes even more imperative. However, I am unfortunate to be an apprentice, and I do not have the status to solicit donations. Reflecting on my financial situation, as described above, I am in a difficult position. Although my heart is filled with a desire to help, I lack the means to provide assistance, which is truly shameful. Alas! In this distorted society where power and wealth dominate, only dignitaries and wealthy individuals can easily raise five or ten thousand at a moment's notice with a mere word. If someone of my humble status sincerely begs for help, who will care? Who will consider the plight of the many victims? Since ancient times, friends with tight finances and frugal habits are inevitably few, and even if there are one or two who care, they are in the same situation, unable to offer substantial help. Sending the donation booklet back as is would be a heavy burden on my conscience. Moreover, how would I face my hometown in the future? Therefore, I am worried day and night, more so than if I were there myself. Sir, you are a great benefactor who helps people achieve good things. I implore you to provide guidance on how to use what method to make this donation booklet, which many lives rely upon, be successful in meeting its purpose. Please advise me.

Sincerely,

Cheng Lie-fu

Editor's Note: Compassion exists in everyone's heart. However, "viewing others' hunger as one's own hunger and others' drowning as one's own drowning" is merely an exaggeration. In reality, how many people truly have such feelings? Therefore, most ordinary people adopt a policy of "self first" and "love your family and extend it to others."

Now that your hometown has suffered a flood, affecting your family, the most important thing is to find ways to help your family. If you can do it without relying on public assistance, you will be leaving more resources for the public to help other victims. As for raising funds for relief, it is certainly a good thing, but it is the obligation of those who have surplus resources. You do not need to force yourself.

In this society where poverty is widespread, it is normal not to be able to donate money. There is no need to lose face or be ashamed to return to your hometown. Although you cannot donate money, the fact that you do not need help yourself means you are not extremely poor. Moreover, even if you are truly destitute, there is no shame in it. It is only disgraceful to exploit the situation, raise money for personal gain, and fail to account for it later.

Drama

War and Peace (12)

— Ling He

Scene 1: Life and Death

Soldier Geng: Reporting to the company commander, the person is here.

Platoon Leader: Bring a few more lamps from inside.

Company Commander: What's your name?

Youth: My name is Wu Chunshan. I escaped from Youbeikou. Here's a letter, please take a look, sir. (Takes out a letter from his torn clothes. Also, a packet of silver coins.) And forty yuan.

(The Company Commander reads the letter, playing with the silver, seemingly wanting to confiscate the money.)

Youth: Since Youbeikou was taken by the Japanese soldiers, more than half of the houses in our village have been burned down. Many people have also been killed. We are hoping that the Sir will send troops to counterattack, drive back the Japanese soldiers, and save the lives of our people. We are all desperately poor. We managed to scrape together forty yuan, so that the brothers can buy cigarettes and food on the road. Although it is a very small amount, it is truly our heartfelt offering. Please don't laugh at us.

Company Commander: Is that so? Good. (Puts the money into his pocket) Tomorrow I'll talk to the division commander. You can go back now. It's nothing, let him go back. (The Company Commander leaves, followed by the Platoon Leader. The youth is stunned. The soldiers also look at each other.) (No one speaks, silence. About three minutes pass.)

Soldier Yi: (Imitating the Company Commander's actions and tone) Is that so? Good. Tomorrow I'll talk to the division commander. You can go back now. It's nothing, let him go back.

Everyone: Hahahahaha.

Soldier Jia: Damn it, convenience, a moment later it's forty.

Youth: Is our money going to be lost?

Soldier Geng: Who knows?

Everyone: Hahahaha (bitterly laughs)

Soldier Jia: You owe it to this fool! You have too much money. (Suddenly, there are violent cannon sounds, machine gun sounds.)

Soldier Yi: What's happening? Are they attacking? (Another sound)

Soldier Geng: We've already retreated, are they still attacking? (Rifle sounds) Listen, you can hear the gun sounds.

Soldier Wu: It's really getting close. (Soldier Jia is the first to lie down, preparing to fire, the rest follow suit.)

Soldier Jia: Tell them all to come out, now is the time to fight for our lives! (Gunshots get closer and denser)

Soldier Ding: We retreated one hundred and fifty li in one day, that's considered fast running, are they really going to chase us? (Bugle sounds, it's an emergency assembly order.)

Platoon Leader: (Rushing in.) Quick! Everyone line up.

(With one command, everyone stands up)

Soldier Ding: Platoon leader! What's going on?

Platoon Leader: Quick! Quick! The Japanese soldiers are attacking again.

Soldier Yi: Then why aren't we counterattacking?

Soldier Geng: What's going on now? Are we retreating again?

Soldier Jia: Aren't we counterattacking? Are we really just waiting to die?

Platoon Leader: No questions. There are orders from above. Retreat. Quick!

(Two of the loudest cannons fire, shells landing in the middle of the soldiers. Flames, black smoke, dust flying. Cries, shouts, gunfire. Black smoke spreads from the stage to the audience. The curtain slowly falls.)

End of Scene 1, to be continued.
